$\mathrm{C_{10}H_{15}N O}.$ HCl: 201.69  

(1 R,2 S)-2-(Methylamino)-1-phenylpropan-1-ol hydrochloride [ 50-98-6 ]  

Ephedrine Hydrochloride, when dried, contains NLT $99.0\%$ and NMT $101.0\%$ of ephedrine hydrochloride $\mathrm{(C_{10}H_{15}N O{\cdot}H C l)}$ ).  

Description Ephedrine Hydrochloride occurs as white crystals or a crystalline powder.  

It is freely soluble in water, soluble in ethanol(95), slightly soluble in acetic acid(100), and practically insoluble in acetic anhydride or acetonitrile.  

Identification (1) Determine the absorption spectra of aqueous solutions of Ephedrine Hydrochloride and ephedrine hydrochloride RS (1 in 2000) as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavelength. (2) Determine the infrared spectra of Ephedrine Hydrochloride and ephedrine hydrochloride RS as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Midinfrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

(3) An aqueous solution of Ephedrine Hydrochloride (1 in 15) responds to the Qualitative Analysis for chloride.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $-33.0^{\circ}$ and $-36.0^{\circ}$ (after drying, $1\;\mathrm{g}$ , water, $20\;\mathrm{mL}$ ,$100\;\mathrm{mm}$ ).  

Melting point Between 218 and $222\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ $\mathbf{pH}$ Dissolve $1.0\;\mathrm{g}$ of Ephedrine Hydrochloride in $20~\mathrm{mL}$ of water; the pH of this solution is between 4.5 and 6.5. Purity (1) Clarity and color of solution —Dissolve $0.5~\mathrm{g}$ of Ephedrine Hydrochloride in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of water; the solution is colorless and clear.  

(2) Acidity and Alkalinity —Weigh accurately $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of  Ephedrine Hydrochloride, dissolve in $20\;\mathrm{mL}$ of water, and add 1 drop of methyl red TS. Add $0.01\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ of sulfuric acid until the solution turns red if the solution exhibits a yellow color; the amount used of sulfuric acid is NMT $0.10\,\mathrm{~mL~}$ . Add $0.02\,\mathrm{\mol/L}$ of sodium hydroxide solution until the solution turns yellow if the solution exhibits a pink color; the amount used of the sodium hydroxide solution is NMT $0.20\,\mathrm{mL}$ .  

(3) Sulfate —Dissolve $50~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ephedrine Hydrochloride in $40~\mathrm{mL}$ of water, add $1\ \mathrm{mL}$ of dilute hydrochloric acid and $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of barium chloride TS and allow to stand for 10 minutes; the solution remains unchanged.  

(4) Heavy metals —Proceed with $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Ephedrine Hydrochloride as directed under Method 2 and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $1.0\ \mathrm{mL}$ of lead standard solution $\left\langle10\,\mathrm{ppm}\right\rangle$ .  

(5) Related substances —Dissolve $50~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ephedrine Hydrochloride in $50\;\mathrm{mL}$ of mobile phase and use this solution as the test solution. Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add the mobile phase to it make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions. Determine the peak area obtained from each solution as directed in the automatic integration method; the sum of peak areas other than the major peak area from the test solution is not greater than the major peak area from the standard solution.  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $210\;\mathrm{nm})$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4.6~\mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and $15~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography ( $\ensuremath{\left\langle5\;\ensuremath{\upmu\mathrm{m}}\right.\right.}$ in particle diameter).   
Column temperature: A constant temperature of about $45\,^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  
Mobile phase: A mixture of sodium lauryl sulfate solution (1 in 128), acetonitrile and phosphoric acid $(640:360:1)$ ).   
Flow rate: Adjust so that the retention time of  

ephedrine is about 14 minutes.  

# System suitability  

Test for required detectability: Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of the standard solution and add the mobile phase to make 20 mL. Confirm that the peak area of ephedrine obtained from $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of this solution is equivalent to $4\%$ to $6\%$ of that of ephedrine from the standard solution.  

System performance: Dissolve $1~\mathrm{mg}$ of ephedrine hydrochloride RS and $4~\mathrm{mg}$ of atropine sulfate in $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ of diluted methanol (1 in 2). Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of this solution according to the above operating conditions; ephedrine and atropine are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 1.5.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times according to the above operating conditions with $10\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solution; the relative standard deviation of the peak areas of ephedrine is NMT $2.0\%$ .Time span of measurement: About 3 times the retention time of ephedrine after the solvent peak.  

Loss on drying NMT $0.5\%$ $\mathrm{~\,~1~g,~}105\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ , 3 hours). Residue on ignition NMT $0.1\%$ ($\mathrm{~\textit~{~1~g~}~}$ Assay Weigh accurately about $0.4~\mathrm{g}$ of Ephedrine Hydrochloride, previously dried, dissolve in $50\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of a mixture of acetic anhydride and acetic acid(100) $(7:3)$ by warming. After cooling, titrate with $0.1\,\mathrm{\mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS (potentiometric titration under the Titrimetry). Perform a blank test in the same manner and make any necessary correction.  

Each mL of $0.1\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS $=20.169\;\mathrm{mg}$ of $\mathrm{C_{10}H_{15}N O}.$ ·HCl  

Packaging and storage Preserve in well-closed containers.  

# Ephedrine Hydrochloride Injection 에페드린염산염주사액  

Ephedrine Hydrochloride Injection is an aqueous injection and contains NLT $95.0\%$ and NMT $105.0\%$ of the labeled amount of ephedrine hydrochloride $(\mathrm{C_{10}H_{15}N O}\cdot\mathrm{HCl}:201.69)$ .  

Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Injections, with Ephedrine Hydrochloride.  

Description Ephedrine Hydrochloride Injection occurs as a clear, colorless liquid.   
$p H$ —Between 4.5 and 6.5.  

Identification Take an amount of Ephedrine Hydrochloride Injection equivalent to $509~\mathrm{mg}$ of ephedrine hydrochloride according to the labeled amount, and add water to make $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ . Determine the absorption spectra of this solution as directed under Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; it exhibits maxima between $249~\mathrm{nm}$ and $253~\mathrm{nm}$ , between $255~\mathrm{nm}$ and $259\;\mathrm{nm}$ , and between $261~\mathrm{nm}$ and 265 nm.  

Sterility Meets the requirements. Bacterial endotoxins Less than 7.5 EU per mg of ephedrine hydrochloride.  

Particulate contamination: Visible particles Meets the requirements.  

Insoluble particulate matter in injections Meets the requirements.  

Extractable volume of injections Meets the requirements.  

Assay Pipet an amount of Ephedrine Hydrochloride Injection equivalent to about $40~\mathrm{{mg}}$ of ephedrine hydrochloride $\mathrm{\left(C_{10}H_{15}N O{\cdot}H C l\right)}$ , add exactly $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, then add water to make $200~\mathrm{mL}$ ,and use this solution as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $40~\mathrm{mg}$ of ephedrine hydrochloride RS, previously dried at $105~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 3 hours, dissolve in exactly $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, then add water to make exactly $200~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the peak area ratios, $Q_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $Q_{S}$ , of ephedrine to the peak area of the internal standard, respectively.  

Internal standard solution —Etilefrine hydrochloride solution (1 in 500).  

# Operating conditions  

For the detector, column, column temperature, mobile phase and flow rate, proceed as directed under the operating conditions under the Purity (5) of Ephedrine Hydrochloride.  

# System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the internal standard and ephedrine are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 1.5.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solution under the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratios of ephedrine to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, hermetic containers.  

# $10\%$ Ephedrine Hydrochloride Powder 에페드린염산염10배산  

Ephedrine Hydrochloride $10\%$ Ephedrine Hydrochloride  

$10\%$ Ephedrine Hydrochloride Powder contains NLT $9.3\%$ and NMT $10.7\%$ of ephedrine hydrochloride $(\mathrm{C_{10}H_{15}N O}\cdot\mathrm{HCl}:201.69)$ .  

# Method of preparation  

Ephedrine hydrochloride  

$100\;\mathrm{g}$  

Prepare as directed under Powders, with the above. Identification Take $0.5\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of $10\%$ Ephedrine Hydrochloride Powder, add $100\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of water, shake for 20 minutes and filter. Determine the absorption spectrum of the filtrate as directed under Ultraviolet-visible Spectrophotometry: it exhibits maxima between $249~\mathrm{nm}$ and 253 nm, between $255~\mathrm{nm}$ and $259\ \mathrm{nm}$ and between $261\ \mathrm{nm}$ and $265\ensuremath{\,\mathrm{\nm}}$ . Determine the absorption spectrum of the filtrate as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; it exhibits maxima between $249\ \mathrm{nm}$ and $253\,\mathrm{\nm}$ ,between $255~\mathrm{nm}$ and $259\ \mathrm{nm}$ , and between $261\ \mathrm{nm}$ and $265~\mathrm{nm}$ .  

# Particle size distribution estimation by analytical sieving Meets the requirements.  

Uniformity of dosage units (distribution) Meets the requirements.  

Assay Weigh accurately about $0.4~\mathrm{g}$ of $10\%$ Ephedrine Hydrochloride Powder, add $150~\mathrm{mL}$ of water and extract with the aid of ultrasonicator for 10 minutes with occasional shaking. Shake more for 10 minutes, add exactly $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution and water to make $200\,\mathrm{\mL}$ , centrifuge and use the supernatant as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $40\,\mathrm{~mg~}$ of Ephedrine Hydrochloride RS, previously dried at $105~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 3 hours, put exactly to $10\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of internal standard solution to dissolve, add water to make $200~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test and the standard solution as directed under Liquid Chromatography according to the following condition and calculate the ratios, QT and QS, of the peak area of ephedrine to that of the internal standard of each solution.  

Amount (mg) of ephedrine hydrochloride $(\mathrm{C_{10}H_{15}N O{\cdot}H C l})$ $=$ Amount (mg) of ephedrine hydrochloride $\mathrm{RS}{\times}\,\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}$ Internal standard solution —Etilefrine hydrochloride solution (1 in 500).  

# Operating conditions  

Follow the operating conditions under the Purity (4) of Ephedrine Hydrochloride for the detector, column, column temperature, mobile phase and flow rate.  

System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the internal standard and ephedrine are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 1.5.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution under the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratio of ephedrine to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in well-closed containers.  

# Ephedrine Hydrochloride Tablets 에페드린염산염정  

Ephedrine Hydrochloride Tablets contain NLT $93.0\%$ and NMT $107.0\%$ of the labeled amount of ephedrine hydrochloride $\mathrm{{(C_{10}H_{15}N O{\cdot}H C l{:}201.69)}}$ .  

Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Tablets, with Ephedrine Hydrochloride.  

Identification Weigh an amount of Ephedrine Hydrochloride Tablets, previously powdered, equivalent to 50 mg of ephedrine hydrochloride according to the labeled amount, add $100~\mathrm{mL}$ of water, shake for 20 minutes to mix, and then filter. Determine the absorption spectrum of the filtrate as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; it exhibits maxima between $249\,\mathrm{\Omeganm}$ and $253\ \mathrm{nm}$ , between $255~\mathrm{nm}$ and $259\ \mathrm{nm}$ , and between 261 nm and $265~\mathrm{nm}$ .  

Dissolution Perform the test with 1 tablet of Ephedrine Hydrochloride Tablets at 50 revolutions per minute according to Method 2 under the Dissolution, using $900\;\mathrm{mL}$ of water as the dissolution medium. Take $20~\mathrm{mL}$ or more of the dissolved solution 30 minutes after starting the test, and filter through a membrane filter with a pore size of NMT $0.45~{\upmu\mathrm{m}}$ . Discard the first $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the filtrate, and use the subsequent filtrate as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $28~\mathrm{mg}$ of ephedrine hydrochloride RS, previously dried at $105\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 3 hours, and dissolve in water to make exactly $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $5\;\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add water to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the peak areas, $A_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $A_{S}$ , of ephedrine, respectively. The acceptable dissolution criterion is NLT $80\%$ of Ephedrine Hydrochloride Tablets dissolved in 30 minutes.  

Dissolution rate $(\%)$ of the labeled amount of ephedrine $(\mathrm{C_{10}H_{15}N O{\cdot}H C l})$  

$=$ Amount (mg) of the ephedrine RS taken $\times\frac{A_{\mathrm{T}}}{A_{\mathrm{S}}}\times\frac{1}{C}\times90$  

$C$ :Labeled amount (mg) of ephedrine $(\mathrm{C_{10}H_{15}N O{\cdot}H C l})$ ) in 1 tablet.  

Operating conditions  

Ephedrine Hydrochloride: Perform the test according to the operating conditions under the Purity (5) Related substances.  

System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the number of theoretical plates and the symmetry factor of the peak of ephedrine are NLT 10000 and NMT 2.0, respectively.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $10\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solutions according to the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak areas of ephedrine is NMT $2.0\%$ .  

# Uniformity of dosage units Meets the requirements.  

Assay Weigh accurately the mass of NLT 20 tablets of Ephedrine Hydrochloride Tablets, and powder. Weigh accurately an amount, equivalent to about $40~\mathrm{~mg}$ of ephedrine hydrochloride $(\mathsf{C}_{10}\mathrm{H}_{15}\mathrm{NO}{\cdot}\mathrm{HCl})$ , add $150\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of water, sonicate for 10 minutes while occasionally shaking to mix, and shake for 10 minutes to mix. Then, add exactly $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, and then add water to make $200\;\mathrm{mL}$ . Centrifuge this solution, and use the clear supernatant as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $40~\mathrm{mg}$ of ephedrine hydrochloride RS, previously dried at $105~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 3 hours, dissolve exactly $10\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of the internal standard solution, then add water to make $200~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the peak area ratios, $Q_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $Q_{S}$ , of ephedrine to the peak area of the internal standard, respectively.  

$=$ Amount (mg) of ephedrine hydrochloride $\mathrm{RS}{\times}\,\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}$ Internal standard solution —Etilefrine hydrochloride solution (1 in 500).  

# Operating conditions  

For the detector, column, column temperature, mobile phase and flow rate, proceed as directed under the operating conditions in the Purity (4) under Ephedrine Hydrochloride.  

# System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the internal standard and ephedrine are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 1.5.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution under the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratios of ephedrine to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in well-closed containers.  

![](images/9ae511d5282ae1a9ab40c396ba8c699d0dcb8546e63e1051ccb6ceeaae59d6a2.jpg)  

Adrenaline   
Epirenamine $\mathrm{C}9\mathrm{H}_{13}\mathrm{NO}_{3}$ : 183.20 4-[(1 R)-1-Hydroxy-2-(methylamino)ethyl]benzene-1,2- diol [ 51-43-4 ]  
Epinephrine, when dried, contains NLT $98.0\%$ and NMT $101.0\%$ of epinephrine $\left({\bf C}_{9}{\bf H}_{13}{\bf N O}_{3}\right)$ .Description Epinephrine occurs as a white to grayish white crystalline powder and is odorless.   
It is freely soluble in acetic acid(100), very slightly soluble in water, and practically insoluble in methanol, ethanol(95) or ether.   
It dissolves in dilute hydrochloric acid.   
It is gradually changed to brown by air or light.  

Identification (1) Dissolve $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of Epinephrine in 10 mL of diluted ethanol (1 in 500) and use this solution as the test solution. To $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of the test solution, add $4~\mathrm{mL}$ of water and 1 drop of iron(III) chloride TS; the resulting solution exhibits dark green and then slowly turns red.  

(2) Take $1~\mathrm{mL}$ each of the test solution in (1) in test tubes A and B, respectively, add $10\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of potassium hydrogen phthalate buffer solution $(\mathrm{pH}\ 3.5)$ to the test tube A and add $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of phosphate buffer solution (pH 6.5) to the test tube B, add $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of iodine TS to the test tubes A and B, respectively, allow them to stand for 5 minutes, then add $2~\mathrm{mL}$ of sodium thiosulfate TS to each test tube; the test tube A exhibits red and the test tube B develops deep red color.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $-50.0^{\circ}$ and $-53.5^{\circ}$ $\mathrm{~\textit~{~1~g~}~}$ ,after drying, 1 mol/L hydrochloric acid TS, $25~\mathrm{mL}$ , 100 mm).  

Purity (1) Clarity and color of solution —Dissolve $0.1~\mathrm{g}$ of Epinephrine in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of dilute hydrochloric acid; the solution is clear and the color is not more intense than that of the Color Matching Fluid A.  

(2) Adrenalone —Dissolve $50~\mathrm{mg}$ of Epinephrine in $0.05\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ hydrochloric acid TS to make exactly $25~\mathrm{mL}$ ,and perform the test as directed under the Ultravioletvisible Spectroscopy; the absorbance at a wavelength of $310\;\mathrm{nm}$ is NMT 0.40.  

(3) Norepinephrine —Weigh $10.0~\mathrm{mg}$ of Epinephrine, dissolve in $2.0\ \mathrm{mL}$ of a solution of L-tartaric acid in methanol (1 in 200). Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, and add $3.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of pyridine. Add $1.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of freshly prepared sodium naphthoquinone sulfonate TS, allow to stand for 30 minutes in the dark, and add $5.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of pyridine containing $50~\mathrm{mg}$ of L-ascorbic acid to the resulting solution; the color of the solution is not more intense than that of the control solution.  

Control solution —Dissolve $2.0~\mathrm{mg}$ of norepinephrine tartrate RS and $90~\mathrm{mg}$ of epinephrine tartrate RS in methanol to make exactly $10\,\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, and proceed in the same manner.  

Loss on drying NMT $1.0\%$ ($\,2~\mathrm{g}$ , in vacuum, silica gel, 18 hours).  

# Residue on ignition NMT $0.1\%$ ($\mathrm{~\textit~{~1~}~}\mathrm{g})$  

Assay Weigh accurately about $0.3\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of Epinephrine, previously dried, dissolve in $50~\mathrm{mL}$ of acetic acid(100), and titrate with $0.1\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS (indicator: 2 drops of methylrosaniline chloride TS). Perform a blank test in the same manner and make any necessary correction.  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, tight containers. Store at a cold place under nitrogen atmosphere.  

# Epinephrine Injection 에피네프린주사액  

Adrenaline Hydrochloride Injection   
Epirenamine Hydrochloride Injection   
Epinephrine Hydrochloride Injection   
Epinephrine Injection is an aqueous solution for injection and contains NLT $0.085~\mathrm{w/v}\%$ and NMT 0.115 $\mathrm{w}/\mathrm{v}\%$ of epinephrine (C9H13NO3: 183.20).  

Preparation Prepare as directed under Injections, with Epinephrine by dissolving in diluted hydrochloric acid (9 in 10000).  

Description Epinephrine Injection occurs as a clear, colorless liquid.   
It is gradually changed to pale red and then brown by air or light.   
$p H$ —Between 2.3 and 5.0.  

Identification (1) Add $4~\mathrm{mL}$ of water and 1 drop of iron(III) chloride TS to $1\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of Epinephrine Injection; the solution turns dark green and slowly changes to red. (2) Take $1~\mathrm{mL}$ each of Epinephrine Injection in test tubes A and B and perform the test as directed under the Identification (2) under Epinephrine.  

Sterility Meets the requirements. Bacterial endotoxins Less than 357.0 EU per mg of epinephrine.  

Particulate contamination: Visible particles Meets the requirements.  

Insoluble particulate matter in injections Meets the requirements.  

Extractable volume of injections Meets the requirements.  

Assay Pipet $30~\mathrm{mL}$ of Epinephrine Injection, transfer to a separatory funnel, add $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of carbon tetrachloride, and shake vigorously to mix for 1 minute. Allow to stand, and discard the carbon tetrachloride layer. Repeat this procedure 3 times. Wash the stopper and inlet of the separatory funnel with a small amount of water, and introduce $0.2~\mathrm{mL}$ of starch TS. While shaking, add iodine TS dropwise until the solution exhibits a persistent blue color, then immediately add sodium thiosulfate TS dropwise until the blue color disappears. Add $2.1\ \mathrm{g}$ of sodium bicarbonate to the liquid, preventing it from coming in contact with the inlet of the separatory funnel, and shake until most of the sodium bicarbonate dissolves. To this solution, immediately add $1.0\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of acetic anhydride. Immediately stopper the separatory funnel loosely and allow to stand until the evolution of gas ceases. Shake vigorously, allow to stand for 5 minutes, extract six times with $25~\mathrm{mL}$ volumes of chloroform. Filter each chloroform extract using cotton wool. Combine all chloroform extracts, evaporate on a steam bath to $3\;\mathrm{mL}$ with a current of air. Transfer this residue by means of small portions of chloroform to a tared beaker and heat again to evaporate to dryness. Dry the residue at $105\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 30 minutes, cool in a desiccator (silica gel), weigh accurately the weight, W (mg), of the dried residue, and dissolve in chloroform to make exactly $5\;\mathrm{mL}$ . Determine the optical rotation, α D,using a $100{\-}\mathrm{mm}$ cell as directed under the Optical Rotation.  

$$
=\,0.5923\times W\times\dot{\left(0.5+}\frac{0.5\times\upalpha_{\mathrm{D}}}{93}\right)
$$  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, hermetic containers. Colored containers may be used for Epinephrine Injection.  

# Epirubicin Hydrochloride 에피루비신염산염  

![](images/3b76ddfc449d64b68a7f46a16ee051fda3f60d690d8fc070b6664fc364eb3cf3.jpg)  

$\mathrm{C}_{27}\mathrm{H}_{29}\mathrm{NO}_{11}$ ·HCl: 579.98 (8R,10S)-10-((2S,4S,5R,6S)-4-Amino-5-hydroxy-6-methyltetrahydro-2H-pyran-2-yl)-6,8,11-tri-hydroxy-8- (2-hydroxyacetyl)-1-methoxy-7,8,9,10- tetrahydrotetracene-5,12-dione hydrochloride [ 56390-09- 1 ]Epirubicin Hydrochloride is the hydrochloride of a derivative of daunorubicin. Epirubicin Hydrochloride contains NLT $970~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ and NMT $1020~\mathrm{\upmug}$ (potency) of epirubicin hydrochloride $(\mathrm{C}_{27}\mathrm{H}_{29}\mathrm{NO}_{11}\cdot\mathrm{HCl})$ per mg, calculated on the anhydrous and solvent-free basis.  

Description Epirubicin Hydrochloride occurs as a pale yellowish red to brownish red powder.   
It is soluble in water or methanol, slightly soluble in ethanol(95) and practically insoluble in acetonitrile.   
It is hygroscopic.  

Identification (1) Determine the absorption spectra of solutions of Epirubicin Hydrochloride and epirubicin hydrochloride RS in methanol (3 in 200000) as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavelengths.  

(2) Determine the infrared spectra of Epirubicin Hydrochloride and epirubicin hydrochloride RS as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $+310^{\circ}$ and $+340^{\circ}$ (10 mg calculated on the anhydrous and solvent-free basis, methanol, $20\;\mathrm{mL}$ ,$100\;\mathrm{mm}$ ).  

$\mathbf{pH}$ Dissolve $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of Epirubicin Hydrochloride in $2\;\mathrm{mL}$ of water; the pH of this solution is between 4.0 and 5.5. Absorbance $E_{1c m}^{1\%}$ ($495\ \mathrm{nm})$ ): 200 to 230 ( $15~\mathrm{mg}$ calculated on the anhydrous and solvent-free basis, methanol, $1000\;\mathrm{mL}$ ).  

Purity (1) Clarity and color of solution —Dissolve 50 mg of Epirubicin Hydrochloride in $5\ \mathrm{mL}$ of water; the solution is clear and dark red.  

(2) Heavy metals —Proceed with $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Epirubicin Hydrochloride as directed under Method 2 and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $2.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of lead standard solution (NMT 20 ppm).  

(3) Related substances —Weigh accurately an amount equivalent to $50~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) of Epirubicin Hydrochloride, dissolve in the internal standard solution to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Use this solution as the test solution. Take $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the test solution and perform the test as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions. Determine each peak area as directed in the automatic integration method and calculate the total peak area of substances other than epirubicin and 2-naphthalenesulfonic acid by the percentage peak area method; it is NMT $5.0\%$ .  

Internal standard solution —A solution of sodium 2- naphthalenesulfonate in a mixture of water, acetonitrile, methanol and phosphoric acid $(540:290:170:1)$ ) (1 in 2000).  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $254\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4\,\textrm{m m}$ in internal diameter and about $25~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with trimethylsilyl silica gel for liquid chromatography ( $\left(6~\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Column temperature: A constant temperature of about $35\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  

Mobile phase: Dissolve $2{\mathrm{~g~}}$ of sodium lauryl sulfate in a mixture of water, acetonitrile, methanol and phosphoric acid $(540:290:170:1)$ to make $1000\;\mathrm{mL}$ .  

Flow rate: Adjust so that the retention time of epirubicin is about 9.5 minutes.  

# System suitability  

Test for required detectability: Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of the test solution, add the mobile phase to make exactly 100 mL, and use this solution as the system suitability solution (1). Pipet $1.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution and add the mobile phase to make exactly $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ . Confirm that the peak area of epirubicin obtained from $10\,\mathrm{\upmuL}$ of this solution is equivalent to $7\%$ to $13\%$ of that obtained from $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the system suitability solution (1).  

System performance: Weigh $50~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) of epirubicin hydrochloride RS and dissolve in the internal standard solution to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Use this solution as the system suitability solution (2). Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of this solution according to the above conditions; the internal standard and epirubicin are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 20.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 5 times with $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ each of the system suitability solutions (2) according to the above conditions; the relative standard deviation of the ratios of the peak area of epirubicin to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Time span of measurement: About 3 times the retention time of epirubicin after the solvent peak.  

(4) Residual solvent —Weigh accurately about $0.3~\mathrm{g}$ of Epirubicin Hydrochloride, add exactly $0.6~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, dissolve in dimethylacetamide to make $6~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use it as the test solution. Separately, pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol, add dimethylacetamide to make exactly $25~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard stock solution. Pipet $125~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of acetone, $30~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of ethanol(99.5), $32\ \upmu\mathrm{L}$ of 1-propanol, and $17\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard stock solution each, add exactly $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, then add dimethylacetamide to make $100\ \mathrm{mL}$ .Use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $1~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the ratios, $Q_{\mathrm{Ta}}$ and $Q_{\mathrm{Sa}}$ ,$Q_{\mathrm{Tb}}$ and $Q_{\mathrm{Sb}}$ ,$Q_{\mathrm{Tc}}$ and $Q_{\mathrm{Sc}}$ , and $Q_{\mathrm{Td}}$ and $Q_{\mathrm{Sd}}.$ , of peak areas of acetone, ethanol, 1-propanol and methanol to that of the internal standard, respectively. Calculate the amounts of acetone, ethanol, 1-propanol and methanol with the following equation: NMT $1.5\%$ ,NMT $0.5\%$ , NMT $0.5\%$ and NMT $0.1\%$ , respectively.  

$$
\begin{array}{r}{\mathrm{Content}\left(\mathcal{U}\right)\mathrm{of~acetone}=\frac{1}{W_{\mathrm{T}}}\times\frac{Q_{\mathrm{Ta}}}{Q_{\mathrm{Sa}}}\times593}\end{array}
$$  

$$
\begin{array}{r}{\mathrm{Content}\left(\%\right)\mathrm{of~ethanol}=\frac{1}{W_{\mathrm{T}}}\times\frac{Q_{\mathrm{Tb}}}{Q_{\mathrm{Sb}}}\times142}\end{array}
$$  

$$
\begin{array}{r l}{\centering}&{{}\mathrm{Content}\left(\%\right)\mathrm{of~1-propanol}=\frac{1}{W_{\mathrm{T}}}\times\frac{Q_{\mathrm{Tc}}}{Q_{\mathrm{Sc}}}\times154}\end{array}
$$  

Internal standard solution —A solution of toluene in dimethylacetamide (1 in 100).  

# Operating conditions  

Detector: A flame ionization detector Column: A glass column about $0.25\ \mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $30~\mathrm{m}$ in length, packed with $5\%$ phenylmethyl silicone polymer for gas chromatography coated at $0.25\;\upmu\mathrm{m}$ thick.  

Column temperature: Maintain the temperature at $30~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for the first 5 minutes, then raise the temperature at the rate of $2~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ per minute up to $40~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ , and raise at the rate of $25~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ per minute up to $200~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ if necessary. Keep at $200\;^{\circ}\!C$ for 5 minutes.  

Sample injection port temperature: A constant temperature of about $200~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  

Detector temperature: A constant temperature of about $200~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  

Carrier gas: Helium Flow rate: About $1.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ per minute. Split ratio: $1:100$ System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $1~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above operation conditions; acetone, methanol, ethanol, 1-propanol and the internal standard are eluted in this order. The resolution between the peaks of acetone and the internal standard is NLT 30.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $1~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solutions according to the above conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak areas of acetone, methanol, ethanol and 1-propanol is NMT $4.0\%$ each.  

Water NMT $8.0\%$ $\left(0.1\,\mathrm{~g~}\right.$ , volumetric titration, direct titration).  

Residue on ignition NMT $0.5\%$ (0.1 g). Sterility It meets the requirements when used in sterile preparations.  

Bacterial endotoxins It is less than 1.1 EU per mg (potency) of epirubicin when used in the manufacturing of sterile preparations.  

Histamine It meets the requirements when used in manufacturing of sterile preparations. Weigh an appropriate amount of Epirubicin Hydrochloride to prepare an aqueous solution containing $2.0~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) per mL and use the solution as the test solution. The amount of the test solution is $0.5\;\mathrm{mL}$ .  

Assay Weigh accurately about $50~\mathrm{mg}$ each of Epirubicin Hydrochloride and epirubicin hydrochloride RS, dissolve in the mobile phase to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ each, and use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution, respectively. Perform the test with $10\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the ratios, $Q_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $Q_{\mathrm{S}}$ , of the peak area of epirubicin hydrochloride to that of the internal standard.  

Potency $\mathrm{(\upmug)}$ of epirubicin hydrochloride $(\mathbf{C}_{27}\mathbf{H}_{29}\mathbf{NO}_{11}{\cdot}\mathbf{H}\mathbf{C}\mathrm{l})$ $=$ Potency $\left(\upmu\mathrm{g}\right)$ of epirubicin hydrochloride RS $\mathrm{RS}{\times}\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}$ Internal standard solution —A solution of sodium 2- naphthalenesulfonate in a mixture of water, acetonitrile, methanol and phosphoric acid $(540:290:170:1)$ (1 in 2000).  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $254\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4\,\textrm{m m}$ in internal diameter and about $25~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with trimethylsilyl silica gel for liquid chromatography ( $(6~{\upmu\mathrm{m}}$ in particle diameter).  

Column temperature: A constant temperature of about $35\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  

Mobile phase: Dissolve $2{\mathrm{~g~}}$ of sodium lauryl sulfate in a mixture of water, acetonitrile, methanol and phosphoric acid $(540:290:170:1)$ to make $1000\;\mathrm{mL}$ .  

Flow rate: Adjust so that the retention time of epirubicin hydrochloride is about 9.5 minutes.  

System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above operating conditions; the internal standard and epirubicin are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 20.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 5 times with $10\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solutions according to the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the ratios of the peak area of epirubicin to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in tight containers (0 to $5\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C})$ .  

# Epirubicin Hydrochloride Injection 에피루비신염산염주사액  

Epirubicin Hydrochloride Injection contains NLT $90.0\%$ and NMT $120.0\%$ of the labeled amount of epirubicin hydrochloride $(\mathbf{C}_{27}\mathbf{H}_{29}\mathbf{NO}_{11}{\cdot}\mathbf{H}\mathbf{C}1:579.98)$ .  

Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Injections, with Epirubicin Hydrochloride.  

Identification The retention time ratios of the major peaks from the test solution and standard solution obtained under the Assay to the peaks of the internal standard are the same.  

pH Between 2.5 and 3.5. Sterility Meets the requirements. Bacterial endotoxins Less than 1.1 EU per mg (potency) of epirubicin hydrochloride. Weigh an appropriate amount of Epirubicin Hydrochloride Injection, dissolve in water for endotoxin assay to obtain a solution having known concentration of $0.125~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) per mL, and use this solution as the test solution.  

Particulate contamination: Visible particles Meets the requirements.  

Insoluble particulate matter in injections Meets the requirements.  

Extractable volume of injections Meets the requirements.  

Assay Weigh accurately about $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of Epirubicin Hydrochloride Injection according to the labeled potency, dissolve in $4.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of internal standard solution, add the mobile phase to make $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $10~\mathrm{{mg}}$ (potency) of epirubicin hydrochloride RS, dissolve in exactly $4.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, add the mobile phase to make exactly $10~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $5~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography, and calculate the ratios, QT and QS, of the peak area of epirubicin hydrochloride to that of the internal standard.  

Internal standard solution —Weigh $1{\mathrm{~g~}}$ of sodium 2- naphthalenesulfonate and dissolve in a mixture of water and acetonitrile $(69:31)$ to make $500\;\mathrm{mL}$ .  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $254\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4\,\textrm{m m}$ in internal diameter and about $30~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography ($10\;\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: A mixture of water and acetonitrile $(69:31)$ , adjusted the $\mathrm{pH}$ to 2.0 with phosphoric acid.  

Flow rate: Adjust the flow rate so that the retention time of epirubicin hydrochloride is about 10 minutes. System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $5\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the internal standard and epirubicin hydrochloride are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 8.0.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $5~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solution under the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratio of epirubicin to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in hermetic containers.  

# Epirubicin Hydrochloride for Injection 주사용에피루비신염산염  

Epirubicin Hydrochloride for Injection is an injection to be dissolved before use and contains NLT $90.0\%$ and NMT $120.0\%$ of the labeled amount of epirubicin hydrochloride $(\mathbf{C}_{27}\mathbf{H}_{29}\mathbf{NO}_{11}{\cdot}\mathbf{H}\mathbf{C}1:579.98)$ .  

Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Injections, with Epirubicin Hydrochloride.  

Description Epirubicin Hydrochloride for Injection occurs as a red powder or a mass.  

Identification The retention time ratios of the major peaks from the test solution and the standard solution obtained under the Assay to the peak of the internal standard are the same.  

$\mathbf{pH}$ Dissolve Epirubicin Hydrochloride for Injection in water to make $2~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) per mL; the pH of the solution is between 4.5 and 6.0.  

Sterility Meets the requirements. Bacterial endotoxins Less than 1.1 EU per mg (potency) of epirubicin hydrochloride for injection. Weigh an appropriate amount of Epirubicin Hydrochloride for Injection to obtain a solution having known concentration of $0.125~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) per mL using water for endotoxin assay, and use this solution as the test solution.  

Histamine Meets the requirements. Weigh an appropriate amount of Epirubicin Hydrochloride for Injection to obtain an aqueous solution having known concentration of $2.0~\mathrm{mg}$ per mL, and use this solution as the test solution. The amount of test solution is $0.5\;\mathrm{mL}$ .  

Particulate contamination: Visible particles Meets the requirements.  

Insoluble particulate matter in injections Meets the requirements.  

Uniformity of dosage units Meets the requirements. Water NMT $4.0\%$ ($\mathrm{~\ensuremath~{~0.2~\,g~}~}$ , volumetric titration, direct titration).  

Assay Weigh accurately about $10~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) of Epirubicin Hydrochloride for Injection according to the labeled potency, dissolve in the internal standard solution to make exactly $10~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $10~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) of epirubicin hydrochloride RS, dissolve in the internal standard solution to make exactly $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $5~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography, and determine the ratios, QT and QS, of the peak area of epirubicin hydrochloride to that of the internal standard in each solution.  

Potency $\mathrm{(\upmug)}$ of epirubicin hydrochloride $(\mathrm{C}_{27}\mathrm{H}_{29}\mathrm{NO}_{11}{\cdot}\mathrm{HCl})$  

Internal standard solution —Weigh $1\;\mathrm{g}$ of sodium 2- naphthalenesulfonate and dissolved in a mixture of water and acetonitrile $(69:31)$ to make $500\;\mathrm{mL}$ .  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $254\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4\,\textrm{m m}$ in internal diameter and $30~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography (10 $\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: A mixture of water and acetonitrile $(69:31)$ , adjusted the pH to 2.0 with phosphoric acid.  

Flow rate: Adjust the flow rate so that the retention time of epirubicin hydrochloride is about 10 minutes.  

System suitability

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $5~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solution under the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratio of epirubicin to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in hermetic containers.  

![](images/9f0bcdbf26c1a5f27c8bc02c9a26e6aa23f84caa82e18f190ee9a96ae89f7c46.jpg)  

Vitamin $\ensuremath{\mathrm{D}}_{2}$   
Calciferol $C_{28}\mathrm{H}_{44}\mathrm{O}:396.65$ $(5Z,7E,22E)$ -(3 S)-9,10-Seco-5,7,10(19),22-   
ergostatetraen-3-ol [ 50-14-6 ]  
Ergocalciferol contains NLT $97.0\%$ and NMT $103.0\%$ of ergocalciferol $(\mathbf{C}_{28}\mathbf{H}_{44}\,\mathrm{O})$ .  

Description Ergocalciferol occurs as white crystals. It is odorless or has a slightly characteristic odor. It is freely soluble in ethanol(95), chloroform or ether, sparingly soluble in isooctane, and practically insoluble in water.  

It is affected by air or light.  

Melting point —Between 115 and $118\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ [Put Ergocalciferol into a capillary tube, and dry in a desiccator (in vacuum, NMT $2.67\,\mathrm{\kPa})$ for 3 hours, immediately seal the capillary tube and put the tube into a bath fluid, previously heated at a temperature $10~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ lower than the expected melting point, and measure the melting point with heating at a rate of $3^{\circ}\mathbf{C}$ per minute.]  

Identification (1) Dissolve $0.5~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ergocalciferol in 5 mL of chloroform, add $0.3\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of acetic anhydride and $0.1\ \mathrm{mL}$ of sulfuric acid, and shake to mix; the resulting solution exhibits a red color, and rapidly changes through violet and blue to green.  

(2) Determine the infrared spectra of Ergocalciferol and ergocalciferol RS as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $+102^{\circ}$ and $+107^{\circ}$ (0.3 g, ethanol(95), $20~\mathrm{mL}$ ,$100\;\mathrm{mm})$ ). Dissolve Ergocalciferol within 30 minutes after the container has been opened, and determine the rotation within 30 minutes after the solution has been prepared.  

Absorbance $E_{1c m}^{1\%}$ ($265~\mathrm{nm})$ : Between 445 and 485 (10 mg, ethanol(95), $1000\;\mathrm{mL}$ ).  

Purity (1) Ergosterol —Dissolve $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ergocalciferol in $20~\mathrm{mL}$ of diluted ethanol (9 in 10), add a solution of $20~\mathrm{mg}$ of digitonin dissolved in $2.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol (9 in 10), and allow to stand for 18 hours; no precipitate is formed.  

(2) Reducing substances —To $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of a solution of Ergocalciferol in ethanol(99.5) (1 in 100), add $0.5~\mathrm{mL}$ of a solution of blue tetrazolium in methanol (1 in 200) and $0.5\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of a solution of tetramethylammonium hydroxide in ethanol(99.5) (1 in 10), and allow to stand for 5 minutes. After exactly 5 minutes, add $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of acetic acid(100), and use this solution as the test solution. Proceed with $10~\mathrm{{mg}}$ of ethanol(95.5) in the same manner, and use the resulting solution as the blank test solution. Dissolve an appropriate amount of hydroquinone in anhydrous alcohol to make a solution containing $0.2~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ per mL, proceed with this solution in the same manner, and use the resulting solution as the standard solution. Determine the absorption spectra of the test solution and the standard solution, using the blank test solution as the control solution, as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy at the absorbance maximum wavelength around $525~\mathrm{nm}$ ; the absorbance of the test solution is not greater than that of the standard solution.  

Assay Weigh accurately about $30~\mathrm{mg}$ each of Ergocalciferol and ergocalciferol RS and dissolve them in isoctane, respectively, to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $10~\mathrm{mL}$ each of these solutions, add exactly $3\,\mathrm{\ml}$ of the internal standard solution to each, add the mobile phase to make $50\;\mathrm{mL}$ , and use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ to $20~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the ratios $Q_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $Q_{S}$ ,of peak area of ergocalciferol to that of the internal standard from each solution. Perform the procedure quickly avoiding contact with air or other oxidizing agents as much as possible and using light-resistant containers.  

Internal standard solution —A solution of dimethyl phthalate in isooctane (1 in 100).  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $254\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4\,\textrm{m m}$ in internal diameter and $10\ \mathrm{cm}$ to $30~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with silica gel for liquid chromatography $5~{\upmu\mathrm{m}}$ to $10~{\upmu\mathrm{m}}$ in particle diameter).  

Column temperature: A constant temperature of about $20~^{\circ}\mathbf{C}$ .  

Mobile phase: A mixture of hexane and $n$ -amyl alcohol $(997:3)$ .  

Flow rate: Adjust the flow rate so that the retention time of ergocalciferol is about 25 minutes.  

# System suitability  

System performance: Dissolve $15~\mathrm{mg}$ of ergocalciferol RS in $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of isooctane, transfer the resulting solution into a flask, heat in an oil bath under a reflux condenser for 2 hours, and then cool immediately to room temperature. Transfer the cooled solution to a quartz test tube and irradiate with a short-wavelength lamp (main wavelength: $254~\mathrm{nm}$ ) and a long-wavelength lamp (main wavelength: $365~\mathrm{nm}$ ) for 3 hours. To $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add the mobile phase to make $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of this solution according to the above operating conditions; the relative retention times of previtamin $\ensuremath{\mathrm{D}}_{2}$ ,transvitamin $\ensuremath{\mathrm{D}}_{2}$ and tachysterol 2 to that of ergocalciferol are about 0.5, about 0.6 and about 1.1, respectively, and the resolution between previtamin $\ensuremath{\mathrm{D}}_{2}$ and transvitamin $\ensuremath{\mathrm{D}}_{2}$ is NLT 0.7, and the resolution between ergocalciferol and tachysterol 2 is NLT 1.0.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solution according to the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the ratios of the peak area of ergocalciferol to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light -resistant, hermetic containers under nitrogen atmosphere in a cold place.  

# Ergotamine Tartrate 에르고타민타르타르산염  

![](images/d458d44276be80a6762672f2b4ab534768d5b022797474287d53a86e07d3445a.jpg)  
$(\mathrm{C_{33}H_{35}N_{5}O_{5}})_{2}\,\mathrm{C_{4}H_{6}O_{6}}:1313.41$ $(5^{\prime}S)$ -5'-Benzyl-12'-hydroxy-2'-methylergotaman-3',6',18- trione hemitartrate [ 379-79-3 ]  

Ergotamine Tartrate contains NLT $98.0\%$ and NMT $101.0\%$ of ergotamine tartrate $\mathrm{\small{[(C_{33}H_{35}N_{5}O_{5})_{2}{\cdot}C_{4}H_{6}O_{6}]}}$ ,calculated on the dried basis.  

Description Ergotamine Tartrate occurs as a colorless crystal, or a white to pale yellowish white or grayish white crystalline powder.  

It is slightly soluble in water or ethanol(95). Melting point —About $180\,^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ (with decomposition). Identification (1) Dissolve $1~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ergotamine Tartrate in a mixture of acetic acid(100) and ethyl acetate $(1:1)$ ,pipet $0.5~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, shake to mix in cold water, add $0.5\ \mathrm{mL}$ of sulfuric acid, and allow to stand; the resulting solution exhibits a violet color. Add $0.1\,\mathrm{~mL~}$ of diluted iron(III) chloride TS (1 in 12) to the solution; the color of the solution turns blue to bluish purple.  

(2) Dissolve $1~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ergotamine Tartrate in $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of L-tartaric acid (1 in 100). To $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add 2 mL of 4-dimethylaminobenzaldehydeiron(III) chloride TS, and shake to mix; the resulting solution exhibits a blue color.  

Optical rotation Ergotamine base $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between - $155^{\circ}$ and $-165^{\circ}$ . Dissolve $0.35\mathrm{~g~}$ of Ergotamine Tartrate in $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of L-tartaric acid (1 in 100), add $0.5~\mathrm{g}$ of sodium bicarbonate, shake gently and sufficiently to mix, and extract with four $10~\mathrm{mL}$ portions of ethanol-free chloroform. Filter each chloroform extract through a small filter paper, moistened with ethanol-free chloroform, into a 50- mL volumetric flask, allow to stand on a steam bath at $20~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 10 minutes, and add $20~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ ethanol-free chloroform to make $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Determine the optical rotation of this solution in a $100\ \mathrm{mm}$ cell. Pipet $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, and evaporate to dryness in vacuum at below $45\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .Dissolve the residue in $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of acetic acid(100), and titrate with $0.05\,\mathrm{\mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS (indicator: 1 drop of methylosaniline chloride TS). Perform a blank test in the same manner and make any necessary correction. Calculate the specific optical rotation of ergotamine base from the consumed volume of $0.05\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ perchloric acid and the optical rotation.  

Each mL of $0.05\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS $=29.084~\mathrm{mg}$ of $\mathrm{C}_{33}\mathrm{H}_{35}\mathrm{N}_{5}\mathrm{O}_{5}$  

Purity Related substances —Perform this test using light-resistant containers. Weight $40~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ergotamine Tartrate, add exactly $10\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of a solution of L-tartaric acid in diluted methanol (1 in 2) (1 in 1000), dissolve by shaking well to mist, and use the resulting solution as the test solution. Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add a solution of L-tartaric acid in diluted ethanol (1 in 2) (1 in 1000) to make exactly $50\;\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution on the thin-layer chromatographic plate made of silica gel for thin-layer chromatography. Next, develop the plate with a mixture of chloroform and methanol $(9:1)$ as the developing solvent to a distance of about $10~\mathrm{cm}$ , and air-dry the plate. Spray evenly 4-dimethylaminobenzaldehyde TS on the plate; the spots other than the principal spot obtained from the test solution are not more intense than the spots from the standard solution.  

Loss on drying NMT $5.0\%$ $\mathrm{[0.1~g.}$ , in vacuum, $60~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ , 4 hours).  

Assay Weigh accurately about $0.2{\mathrm{~g~}}$ of Ergotamine Tartrate, dissolve in $15~\mathrm{mL}$ of a mixture of acetic acid(100) and acetic anhydride $(50:3)$ , and titrate with $0.05\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS (indicator: 1 drop of methylrosaniline chloride TS). Perform a blank test in the same manner and make any necessary correction.  

Each mL of $0.05\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS $=32.836\;\mathrm{mg}$ of $(\mathrm{C_{33}H_{35}N_{5}O_{5}})_{2}{\cdot}\mathrm{C_{4}H_{6}O_{6}}$ Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, tight containers. Fill the container almost full or replace the air in the empty part with nitrogen and store at below $5\mathrm{{}^{\circ}C}$ .  

# Ergotamine Tartrate Tablets 에르고타민타르타르산염정  

Ergotamine Tartrate Tablets contain NLT $90.0\%$ and NMT $110.0\%$ of the labeled amount of ergotamine tartrate $\mathrm{\small{[(C_{33}H_{35}N_{5}O_{5})_{2}{\cdot}C_{4}H_{6}O_{6}}}$ : 1313.41].  

Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Tablets, with Ergotamine Tartrate.  

Identification Weigh an amount of Ergotamine Tartrate Tablets, previously powdered, equivalent to $5~\mathrm{mg}$ of ergotamine tartrate according to the labeled amount, add 10 mL of hexane, shake for a few minutes to mix, and allow to stand. Then, discard the hexane extracts, add $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of ammonia water(28)-saturated chloroform to the residue, shake for a few minutes to mix, filter, and evaporate the filtrate to dryness on a steam bath. Dissolve the residue with $8\ \mathrm{~mL}$ of a mixture of acetic acid(100) and ethyl acetate $(1:1)$ , take $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, and slowly add $1\ \mathrm{mL}$ of sulfuric acid dropwise while shaking to mix in iced water; the resulting solution exhibits a violet color. To this solution, add $0.1\mod$ of diluted iron(III) chloride TS (1 in 2); the solution turns blue to bluish purple.  

Disintegration It meets the requirements when it is a sublingual tablet. However, the time of the test is 5 minutes.  

Dissolution This test is applicable when it is not a sublingual tablet. Perform the test with 1 tablet of Ergotamine Tartrate Tablets at 75 revolutions per minute according to Method 2 under the Dissolution, using 1000 mL of L-tartaric acid solution (1 in 100) as the dissolution medium. Take the dissolved solution 30 minutes after starting the dissolution test, filter, and use the filtrate as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately an appropriate amount of ergotamine tartrate RS, add the dissolution medium to make the constant concentration, and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Fluorescence Spectroscopy using the dissolution medium as a control solution, and determine the absorbances at an excitation wavelength of $327\ \mathrm{nm}$ and a fluorescence wavelength of $427\;\mathrm{nm}$ .  

It meets the requirements when the dissolution rate of Ergotamine Tartrate Tablets for 30 minutes is NLT $75\%$ .  

Uniformity of dosage units It meets the requirements when the procedure for content uniformity is performed as directed under the Assay.  

Assay Weigh accurately the mass of NLT 20 Ergotamine Tartrate Tablets, and powder. Weigh an amount equivalent to about $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of ergotamine tartrate $[(\mathbf{C}_{33}\mathrm{H}_{35}\mathrm{N}_{5}\mathrm{O}_{5})_{2}$ ·$\mathrm{C_{4}H_{6}O_{6}\mathrm{~J~}}$ , add $50.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution and $300~\mathrm{mL}$ of a mixture of acetonitrile and water $(55:$ 45), sonicate for 10 minutes, and shake to mix. Then, add a mixture of acetonitrile and water $(55:45)$ to make exactly $500~\mathrm{mL}$ , mix, and filter. Discard the first filtrate, and use the subsequent filtrate as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $10~\mathrm{mg}$ ergotamine tartrate RS, previously dried at $60\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ in vacuum for 4 hours, and dissolve in a mixture of acetonitrile and water (55 in 45) to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add $5.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, add a mixture of acetonitrile and water $(55:45)$ to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ ,and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $20~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and calculate the peak area ratios, $Q_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $Q_{S}$ , of ergotamine to the peak area of the internal standard, respectively.  

# $=$ Amount (mg) of ergotamine tartrate $\mathrm{RS}\!\times\!\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}$  

Internal standard solution —Dissolve about $40~\mathrm{mg}$ of ergometrine maleate in a mixture of acetonitrile and water to make $250\;\mathrm{mL}$ .  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $254\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $3.9\ \mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $30~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography (3 to $10\;\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: A mixture of acetonitrile and 0.01 mol/L potassium dihydrogen phosphate solution $\textbf{(55:}$ 45).  

Flow rate: 1 mL/min System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $20~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the symmetry factor of ergotamine is NMT 2.0 with the resolution between the standard solution and the internal standard being NLT 3.0.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $20\,\textrm{\textmu L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratio is NMT $2.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, wellclosed containers.  

Identification (1) Determine the infrared spectra of Ertapenem Sodium and ertapenem sodium RS as directed in the paste method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

(2) Dissolve $0.1\ \mathrm{g}$ (potency) of Ertapenem Sodium in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of water; the resulting solution responds to the Qualitative Analysis (1) for sodium salt.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{405n m}^{25}$ : Between $+216^{\circ}$ and $+238^{\circ}$ ($\mathrm{~\,~}^{1.0~g}$ , calculated on the anhydrous and solvent-free basis, water, $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ ,$100\;\mathrm{mm}$ ).  

Purity (1) Related substance s—Just before starting this test, weigh accurately about $20~\mathrm{~mg~}$ (potency) of Ertapenem Sodium, dissolve in water to make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the test solution. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the test solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the ratios of the peak area of each related substance to total area of the peaks excluding solvent peak from the test solution (ringopened compound: NMT $1.4\%$ ,xazinone: NMT $0.2\%$ ,ProMABA: NMT $0.6\%$ , total dimer: NMT $1.3\%$ , other individual related substances: NMT $0.1\%$ , total related substances: NMT $3.1\%$ ).  

Contents $(\%)$ of individual related substances  

# Ertapenem Sodium 에르타페넴나트륨  

𝑃𝑃𝑃𝑃𝑃𝑃𝑃𝑃 𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎 𝑜𝑜𝑜𝑜 𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖 𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟 𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠 Ertapenem Sodium $\mathrm{C}_{22}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathrm{N}_{3}\mathrm{NaO}_{7}\mathrm{S}$ : 497.50 Sodium 3-({[(2 S,4 S)-4-({(4 R,5 S,6 S)-2-carboxy-6-[(1 R)- 1-hydroxyethyl]-4-methyl-7-oxo-1- azabicyclo[3.2.0]hept-2-en-3-yl}sulfanyl)pyrrolidin-2- yl]carbonyl}amino)benzoate, [ 153773-82-1 ]  

![](images/ebd3430f84741768249347586b3b29743f18a04aa57820af346bd9bf8fc24a8f.jpg)  

Ertapenem Sodium contains NLT $917~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ and NMT $970~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ (potency) of ertapenem $\mathrm{\left(C_{22}H_{25}N_{3}O_{7}S\,:\,475.52\right)}$ per mg, calculated on the anhydrous and solvent-free basis.  

Description Ertapenem Sodium occurs as a white to grayish white powder.  

It is freely soluble in water, and practically insoluble in ethanol.   
It is hygroscopic.  

𝑆𝑆𝑆𝑆𝑆𝑆 𝑜𝑜𝑜𝑜 𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎 𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝 𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎 𝑜𝑜𝑜𝑜ℎ𝑒𝑒𝑒𝑒 𝑡𝑡ℎ𝑎𝑎𝑎𝑎 𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠 ൤൨ 𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝𝑝 𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖 𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡 𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠  

Total content $(\%)$ of related substances $=$ Sum of contents $(\%)$ of all related substances  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $230\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4.6~\mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $25~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with phenylated silica gel for liquid chromatography ( $5~{\upmu\mathrm{m}}$ in particle diameter).  

# Mobile phase  

Mobile phase A: 15 mmol/L sodium phosphate TS $(\mathrm{pH}\,8.0)$ .  

Mobile phase B: Acetonitrile Mobile phase gradient elution conditions   

![](images/a977c82db713a6770b77a9a57bfafbee95e89ba579705f119aa8f45f95ed501f.jpg)  
Flow rate: 1.0 mL/min  

The relative retention time of each related substance peak to the ertapenem peak is as follows.   

![](images/bb44e04b07b0a871fc07da6809afb15f95fd78cfc5931e37bc90cb2c31b9e478.jpg)  

(2) Residual solvent —Weigh accurately about 50 mg (potency) of Ertapenem Sodium, dissolve in water to make exactly $10~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the test solution. Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ each of methyl acetate, methanol, 2- propanol and 1-propanol, add water to make exactly 100 mL, and use this solution as the standard stock solution. Dilute this standard stock solution with water to prepare $0.01\ \mathrm{vol}\%$ and $0.0001\,\;\mathrm{vol}\%$ standard solutions, and use water as a blank test solution. Pipet accurately $1~\mathrm{mL}$ each of the test solution, the standard solution and the blank test solution, transfer them to headspace vials, close with appropriate elastomeric closures, perform the test as directed under the Gas Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the peak areas, $A_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $A_{S}$ , of the residual solvent from the test solution and the standard solution (methyl acetate: NMT $1.3\%$ , methanol: NMT $0.3\%$ , 2-propanol: NMT $0.5\%$ , 1-propanol: NMT $0.1\%$ ).  

$$
=\frac{A_{\mathrm{T}}}{A_{\mathrm{S}}}
$$  

×𝑑𝑑× 𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉𝑉 (%) 𝑜𝑜𝑜𝑜 𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟𝑟 𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠 𝑖𝑖𝑖𝑖 𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠 𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠 𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴𝐴 (𝑔𝑔) 𝑜𝑜𝑜𝑜 𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠𝑠 𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡𝑡 $\times$ Dilution factor of the test solution  

d: Density $(\mathrm{g/mL})$ of residual solvent (methyl acetate: 0.93, methanol and 2-propanol: 0.79, 1-propanol: 0.80)  

Operating conditions  

Detector: A hydrogen flame ionization detector Column: A stainless steel column about $0.32\;\mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $30\textrm{m}$ in length, packed with porous dimethylpolysiloxane for gas chromatography (5 $\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Column temperature: Maintain at $35\ \ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 8 minutes, and then raise to $125\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ at a rate of $50~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ per minute.  

Temperature of injection port: About $180\,^{\circ}\!C$ .  
Temperature of detector: About $250\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  
Carrier gas: Helium   
Conditions of headspace   
Temperature of injection port: $85\,^{\circ}\!C$   
Injection time of test solution: 0.1 minute   
Temperature of needle: $125\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$   
Temperature of conveying port: $135\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$   
Circulation time of gas chromatograph: 20 minutes Constant temperature retention time: 15 minutes Pressurization time: 2.0 minutes  

Sterility It meets the requirements when used in sterile preparations. However, it is excluded in cases where there is a terminal sterilization process in the manufacturing process of sterile preparations.  

Water Between $15.5\%$ and $19.0\%$ $\left(0.1\,\mathrm{~g~}\right.$ , volumetric titration, direct titration).  

Assay Weigh accurately bout $30~\mathrm{~mg~}$ (potency) of Ertapenem Sodium and ertapenem sodium RS at places with the relative humidity of $50\%$ to $60\%$ and NMT $10\%$ ,respectively, dissolve in $10\,\mathrm{\mmol/L}$ 3-( $N$ -morpholine) propanesulfonic acid buffer solution, $\mathrm{pH}\ 7.0$ , and use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution, respectively. Store the test solution and the standard solution at $4\,^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ and use within 18 hours. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the peak areas $A_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $A_{S}$ , of ertapenem from each solution. Potency $(\upmu\mathrm{g})$ of ertapenem $(\mathbf{C}_{22}\mathbf{H}_{25}\mathbf{N}_{3}\mathbf{O}_{7}\mathbf{S})$ )$=$ Potency $(\upmu\mathrm{g})$ of ertapenem sodium $\mathrm{RS}\times\frac{A_{\mathrm{T}}}{A_{\mathrm{S}}}$  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $307\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4.6~\mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $10~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography $\ensuremath{\left\{5\;\upmu\mathrm{m}\right.}}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: Control the mixing ratio of mobile phase A and mobile phase B stepwise or via the gradient elution as follows.  

Mobile phase A: $0.1\%$ phosphoric acid Mobile phase B: Acetonitrile. Mobile phase gradient elution conditions Flow rate: Adjust the flow rate so that the retention time of ertapenem is about 2.5 to 5.0 minutes.

Packaging and storage Preserve in tight containers.  

# Ertapenem Sodium for Injection 주사용에르타페넴나트륨  

Ertapenem Sodium for Injection is an injection, which is dissolved before use, and contains NLT $90.0\%$ and NMT $120.0\%$ of the labeled amount of ertapenem $(\mathbf{C}_{22}\mathbf{H}_{25}\mathbf{N}_{3}\mathbf{O}_{7}\mathbf{S}$ : 475.52).  

Preparation Prepare as directed under Injections, with Ertapenem Sodium.  

Description Ertapenem Sodium for Injection occurs as a white to grayish white powder.  

Identification The retention times of the major peaks obtained from the test solution and standard solution in the Assay are the same.  

$\mathbf{pH}$ Dissolve $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ (potency) of Ertapenem Sodium for Injection in $0.9\%$ sodium chloride injection to make 1 mL; the $\mathrm{pH}$ of this solution is 7.0 to 8.0.  

Purity Related substances —After performing the test as directed under the Assay, calculate as follows from the peak areas for each related substance (ring-opened NMT $10.0\%$ ; oxazinone NMT $1.2\%$ ; total dimers NMT $6.3\%$ ;NMT $0.2\%$ each for other related substances; total related substances NMT $17.5\%$ ).  

Content $(\%)$ of each related substance   
$=(A_{\mathrm{D}}/A_{\mathrm{S}})\times$ amount [mg (potency)] of ertapenem sodium   
$\mathrm{RS}\mid$ {labeled amount [mg (potency) / vial] of ertapenem $\mathrm{sodiuml}\times R R F\}\times100\$ × 100  

$\ensuremath{A_{\mathrm{D}}}$ : Peak area of related substance in test solution $A_{S}$ : Peak area of ertapenem in standard solution RRF : Relative response factor of individual related substance peaks  

![](images/621dd6c3dc55d2e657c74a77d7168aa5baca833f53fb4fba90491f5050b3f29e.jpg)  

Total dimers $(\%)=\mathrm{Sum}$ of amounts $(\%)$ of all dimers (Dimers I, II, III, Ⅴ, Ⅵ, Dimer $\mathrm{IV}+$ Dimer$\cdot\mathrm{H}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{\cdot}$ ). Sterility Meets the requirements. Bacterial endotoxins Ertapenem Sodium for Injection is NMT 0.35 EU per mg (potency) of ertapenem.  

Particulate contamination: Visible particles Meets the requirements.  

Insoluble particulate matter in injections Meets the requirements.  

# Uniformity of dosage units Meets the requirements.  

Water In a location of relative humidity NMT $25\%$ ,without removing the elastomeric closure and metal ring, weigh accurately the entire mass of 1 vial of Ertapenem Sodium for Injection, and inject $20.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of a mixture of methanol and dimethylformamide $(1:1)$ into the vial through a syringe. Shake to mix for 4 to 8 minutes until the sample is completely dissolved, and use a syringe to place the dissolved test solution in $2\,\,1.5\,\,\mathrm{mL}$ test tubes, immediately insert the stoppers, and centrifuge for 2 minutes at 14000 revolutions per minute. From the two test tubes, weigh the clean supernatant and place in vials for gas chromatography. Use these solutions as the test solutions. Evacuate the remaining solution from the vial of Ertapenem Sodium for Injection, wash with methanol and dry, measure the sum of the masses of the vial, elastomeric closure and metal ring, and subtract this sum from the total mass. Use the difference as the amount $(\mathrm{mg})$ of sample. Separately, place $100~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of water each in $100{\-}\mathrm{mL}$ and $200{\mathrm{-mL}}$ volumetric flasks, previously dried for 2 hours at $100~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ and cooled to room temperature before use, and add a mixture of methanol and dimethylformamide $(1:1)$ to the gauge line. Immediately plug with an elastomeric closure and seal, and mix well. Use these solutions as the standard solution (1) $(1~\mathrm{mg/mL})$ and the standard solution (2) $(0.5\mathrm{~mg/mL})$ . Place a mixture of methanol and dimethylformamide $(1:1)$ in a volumetric flask previously dried for 2 hours at $100~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ and cooled to room temperature before use, immediately plug with an elastomeric closure and seal, and use this solution as the blank test solution. Perform the test with $1~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution (1) (1 $\mathrm{{mg/mL})}$ ) as directed under the Gas Chromatography according to the following conditions, and measure the water peak areas, $A_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $A_{S}$ of the test solution and the standard solution (NMT $2.3\%$ ). Use a mixture of methanol and dimethylformamide $(1:1)$ prepared by placing $500~\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol and $500~\mathrm{mL}$ of dimethylformamide in a $1000{\mathrm{-mL}}$ container, mixing well, substituting with nitrogen and sealing.  

Water $(\%)$ in Ertapenem Sodium for Injection $=\left(A_{\mathrm{T}}/\,A_{\mathrm{S}}\right)\times\left(0.1\,/\right.$ amount of sample $(\mathrm{mg}))\times1000$ $\times\,(20\,/\,100)\times100$  

0.1: Amount (mL) of water in the standard solution  

1000: Specific gravity of water $(\mathrm{{mg/mL})}$   
20: Dilution factor of the test solution   
100: Dilution factor of the standard solution  

Operating conditions Detector: Thermal conductivity detector Column: A gas pipe about $0.53\mathrm{~mm}$ in internal diameter and about $25\,\textrm{m}$ in length, packed with porous polystyrene-divinylbenzene copolymer for gas chromatography ( $20\;\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter). Column temperature: Hold at $90~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 5 minutes, heat at a rate of $25~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ per minute to $250~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ , and hold at $250\ \,^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 5 minutes. Re-equilibrate for 1 minute at $90\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ before the next injection.  

Injection port temperature: $200~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ Detector temperature: $250\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ Carrier gas: Helium  

Flow rate: Adjust the flow rate so that the retention time of water is between 1 and 2 minutes.  

Assay Weigh accurately about $20~\mathrm{~mg~}$ (potency) of Ertapenem Sodium for Injection and ertapenem sodium RS, dissolve in the diluent to contain exactly $0.2~\mathrm{mg}$ (potency) per mL. Use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution. Store the test solution and the standard solution at $5{\pm}3\ \,^{\circ}\mathrm{C},$ , and use within 24 hours. Pipet $10\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution, perform the test as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the peak areas, $A_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $A_{S}$ , of ertapenem for each solution.  

Amount [mg (potency)] of ertapenem $(\mathbf{C}_{22}\mathbf{H}_{25}\mathbf{N}_{3}\mathbf{O}_{7}\mathbf{S})$ $=$ Amount [mg (potency)] of ertapenem sodium RS $\times\left(A_{\mathrm{T}}\,/\,A_{\mathrm{S}}\right)$  

Diluent— Mixture of $15~\mathrm{mmol/L}$ 4-morpholine propane sulfonate $(\mathrm{pH}\,7.5)$ and acetonitrile $(9:1)$ .  

4-morpholine propane sulfonate $(p H\,7.5)$ —Dissolve $3.5~\mathrm{g}$ of 4-morpholine propane sulfate in $1000~\mathrm{mL}$ of water, and adjust $\mathrm{pH}$ to 7.5.  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $230\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column $4.6\;\mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and $2.5~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography $(5\,\textrm{\textmu m}$ in  

particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: Control the mixing ratio of mobile phase A and mobile phase B stepwise or via the gradient elution as follows.  

Mobile phase A: $0.1\%$ phosphoric acid $\mathrm{(pH\,8.0)}$ Mobile phase B: Mixture of acetonitrile and $0.1\%$ phosphoric acid $(\mathrm{pH}\,8.0)$ )$(1:3)$ .  

Mobile phase gradient elution conditions Flow rate: 1.0 mL/min  

![](images/21351dca2d7c3462d6aebb685fc8cf4390b685d045e6a85250f045e5f9381fd7.jpg)  

Relative retention time of each related substance   
Packaging and storage Preserve in hermetic containers.
