Estazolam  

8-Chloro-6-phenyl-4 H-\`1,2,4-triazolo[4,3-a]-1,4- benzodiazepine [ 29975-16-4 ]  

Estazolam, when dried, contains NLT $98.5\%$ and NMT $101.0\%$ of estazolam $(\mathbf{C}_{16}\mathbf{H}_{11}\mathbf{C}\mathrm{l}\mathbf{N}_{4})$ ).  

Description Estazolam occurs as a white to pale yellowish white crystals or crystalline powder. It is odorless and has a bitter taste.  

It is soluble in methanol and in acetic anhydride, sparingly soluble in ethanol(95), and practically insoluble in water and in ether.  

Identification (1) Dissolve about $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estazolam in $3\,\textrm{m L}$ of sulfuric acid and examine the solution under ultraviolet light (wavelength of $365\ensuremath{\,\mathrm{\nm}})$ ); the resulting solution exhibits a yellowish green fluorescent color.  

(2) Determine the absorption spectra of the solutions of Estazolam and estazolam RS in $1~\mathrm{mol/L}$ hydrochloric acid (1 in 100000) as directed under Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavelengths.  

(3) Perform the test with Lorazepam as directed under the Flame Coloration (2); it exhibits a green color. Melting point Between 229 and $233\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ Purity (1) Clarity and color of solution —Dissolve about $0.1\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of Estazolam in $10\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of ethanol(95); the resulting solution is colorless and clear.  

(2) Chloride —Dissolve $1.0\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of Estazolam in 10 mL of ethanol(95) by heating, add $40~\mathrm{mL}$ of water, cool with shaking in iced water, allow to stand until it reaches room temperature, and filter. To $30\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the filtrate, add $6~\mathrm{mL}$ of dilute nitric acid and water to make $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Using this solution as the test solution, perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $0.25~\mathrm{mL}$ of $0.01\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ hydrochloric acid and $6\;\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol (NMT $0.015\%$ ). (3) Heavy metals— Proceed with $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Estazolam according to Method 2 and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $2.0\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of lead standard solution $(\mathrm{NMT}\,\,20\,\,\mathrm{ppm})$ ).  

(4) Arsenic— Prepare the test solution with $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Estazolam according to Method 3 and perform the test $(\mathrm{NMT}\ 2\ \mathrm{ppm})$ ).  

(5) Related substances— Dissolve $0.2{\mathrm{~g~}}$ of Estazolam in $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol and use this solution as the test solution. Pipet $1\,\textrm{m L}$ of this solution, add methanol to make exactly $200~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot 10 $\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution on a plate made of silica gel with fluorescent indicator for thin-layer chromatography, develop the plate with a mixture of hexane, chloroform and methanol $(5:3:1)$ as the developing solvent to a distance of about $10~\mathrm{cm}$ , and airdry the plate.  Examine the plate under ultraviolet light (main wavelength: $254\;\mathrm{nm}$ ); the spots other than the principal spot obtained from the test solution are not more intense than the spots from the standard solution.  

Loss on drying NMT $1.0\%$ ($\mathrm{~\,~1~g,~}105\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ , 4 hours). Residue on ignition NMT $0.1\%$ (2 g). Assay Weigh accurately about $0.25~\mathrm{g}$ of Estazolam, previously dried, dissolve in $100\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of acetic anhydride, and titrate with $0.1\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS (potentiometric titration under the Titrimetry). The endpoint of the titration is when the solution changes to the equivalence point 2. Perform a blank test in the same manner and make any necessary correction.  

Each mL of $0.1\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ perchloric acid VS $=14.737\;\mathrm{mg}$ of ${\mathrm{C}}_{16}{\mathrm{H}}_{11}{\mathrm{ClN}}_{4}$  

![](images/a03ac7246b3e3c4c4fac3dd54d597d450403a689e8b411bc977a803401c631ad.jpg)  
Packaging and storage Preserve in well-closed containers.  

Estradiol $\mathrm{C_{18}H_{24}O_{2}}$ : 272.38 (17β)-Eestra-1,3,5(10)-triene-3,17-diol [ 50-28-2 ]Estradiol, when dried, contains NLT $97.0\%$ and NMT $103.0\%$ of Estradiol $\left(\mathbf{C}_{18}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{2}\right)$ .  

Description Estradiol occurs as white crystals or a crystalline powder and is odorless.   
It is freely soluble in 1,4-dioxane, soluble in acetone, sparingly soluble in ethanol(95), slightly soluble in sesame oil and practically insoluble in water.  

Identification (1) Determine the absorption spectra of solutions of Estradiol and estradiol RS, respectively, in ethanol(95) (1 in 20000) as directed under Ultravioletvisible Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavelengths. The difference of absorption maxima in each absorption spectra is NLT $3.0\%$ at about $280\;\mathrm{nm}$ .  

(2) Determine the infrared spectra of Estradiol and estradiol RS as directed in the paste method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $+76.0^{\circ}$ and $+83.0^{\circ}$ $\mathbf{(0.250~g}$ , calculated on the anhydrous basis, ethanol(95),  

25 mL, $100\;\mathrm{mm}$  

# Melting point Between 173 and $179\,^{\circ}\!\mathrm{C}$  

Purity Related substances —Weigh about $70~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estradiol, add a mixture of n-butyl chloride and methanol $(5:1)$ , shake vigorously, add a mixture of n-butyl chloride and methanol $(5:1)$ to make $10~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the test solution. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the test solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions. Determine each peak area by the automatic integration method and calculate the peak area, $A_{\mathrm{i}}$ of each related substance and the total area of all peaks AS by the percentage peak area method; the amount of each related substance is NMT $0.5\%$ , and the total amount of related substances is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

$$
\begin{array}{r}{=100\times\frac{A_{\mathrm{i}}}{A_{\mathrm{S}}}}\end{array}
$$  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $280\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4.6~\mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $25~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with porous silanized silica gel for liquid chromatography (3 $\upmu\mathrm{m}$ to $10\;\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: A mixture of isooctane, n-butyl chloride, and methanol $(45:4:1)$ .  

System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the test solution under the above operating conditions; the resolution between the peaks of estradiol and each related substance is NLT 1.0, and the number of theoretical plates and symmetry factor are NLT 800 and NMT 1.5, respectively.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 5 times according to the above conditions with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution; the relative standard deviation of the peak area of estradiol is NMT $2.0\%$ .  

Water NMT $3.5\%$ $\left(0.5\,\mathrm{~g~}\right.$ , volumetric titration, direct titration).  

Assay Weigh accurately about $0.1~\mathrm{g}$ of Estradiol, previously dried, and dissolve in methanol to make exactly $250~\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add $5.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution and $100~\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol and water to make exactly $200\;\mathrm{mL}$ and use this solution as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately a sufficient amount each of estradiol RS (previously determined water contents) and estrone RS and dissolve separately in methanol to contain about $400\ \upmu\mathrm{g}$ of estradiol and $240~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ of estrone per mL. Pipet $10~\mathrm{mL}$ each of these solutions, add $5.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, $100~\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol and add water to make exactly $200~\mathrm{mL}$ and use these solutions as the standard solutions. Perform the test with $25~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and calculate the peak area ratios, $\mathrm{Q_{T}}$ and $\mathrm{Qs}$ , of estradiol to internal standard, respectively.  

$$
\begin{array}{r}{\mathrm{Amount}\left(\mathrm{mg}\right)\mathrm{of~estradiol}\left(\mathrm{C}_{18}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathrm{O}_{2}\right)}\\ {=5\times C\times\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}\qquad\qquad\qquad}\end{array}
$$  

$C$ : Final concentration of Estradiol in the standard solution $(\upmu\mathrm{g/mL)}$  

Internal standard solution —A solution of ethylparabene in methanol (0.6 in 1000).  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $205\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $3.9\ \mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and $30\;\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography (about $5\;\mathrm{{\mum}}$ to $10\,\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: A mixture of acetonitrile and water $(55:45)$ .  

Flow rate: $1\ \mathrm{mL/min}$ System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $25~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution under the above conditions; the internal standard, estradiol, and estrone are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 2.0.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $25\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratio is NMT $2.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, tight containers.  

# Estradiol Benzoate 에스트라디올벤조에이트  

![](images/0eec3eb4042b175caf013db5ba472c682330d5331f09fa2b3603319170a37db6.jpg)  

${\bf C}_{25}{\bf H}_{28}{\bf O}_{3}$ : 376.49 (17β)-3-Hydroxyestra-1,3,5(10)-trien-3-yl benzoate [ 50- 50-0 ]  

Estradiol Benzoate, when dried, contains NLT $97.0\%$ and NMT $101.0\%$ of estradiol benzoate Description Estradiol Benzoate occurs as a white crystalline powder and is odorless.  

It is sparingly in acetone, slightly soluble in methanol, ethanol(95) and ethanol(95), and practically insoluble in water.  

Identification (1) Add $2~\mathrm{mL}$ of sulfuric acid to $2~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estradiol Benzoate; the resulting solution exhibits a yellowish green color with blue fluorescence. Carefully add $2~\mathrm{mL}$ of water; the color of the solution changes to light orange. (2) Determine the infrared spectra of Estradiol Benzoate and estradiol benzoate RS, previously dried, as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $+54^{\circ}$ and $+58^{\circ}$ (after drying, $0.1~\mathrm{g}$ , acetone, $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ ,$100\;\mathrm{mm}$ ).  

Melting point Between 191 and $198\,^{\circ}\mathbf{C}$ Purity (1) $3,\!I7\!a$ -Estradiol —Dissolve $5.0\,\mathrm{~mg~}$ each of Estradiol Benzoate and estradiol benzoate RS in acetone to make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution, respectively. Put exactly $2~\mathrm{mL}$ each of the test solution and standard solution in separate glass-stoppered test tube, add boiling stones, evaporate the acetone by heating on a steam bath, and dry the residue in a desiccator (in vacuum, phosphorus (V) oxide) for 1 hour. Add $1.0\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of dilute ironphenol TS to each test tube. Stopper the test tubes loosely, heat for 30 seconds on a steam bath, shake on a steam bath for several seconds, and heat for 2 minutes again. After cooling the solutions in ice again for 2 minutes, add $4.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of diluted sulfuric acid (7 in 20) and mix well; the solution obtained from the test solution has no more intense than that from the standard solution.  

(2) Related substances —Dissolve $40~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estradiol Benzoate in $2\;\mathrm{mL}$ of acetone, and use this solution as the test solution. Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add acetone to make exactly $100\,\mathrm{\mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution on the thin-layer chromatographic plate made of silica gel with fluorescent indicator for thin-layer chromatography. Next, develop the plate with a mixture of chloroform and diethylamine $(19:1)$ as the developing solvent to a distance of about $15~\mathrm{cm}$ , and air-dry the plate. Examine the plate under ultraviolet light (main wavelength: $254~\mathrm{nm}$ ); the spots other than the principal spot obtained from the test solution are not more intense than the spots from the standard solution.  

Loss on drying NMT $0.5\%$ ($\mathrm{\Omega}^{0.5{\mathrm{~g~}}}$ , in vacuum, phosphorus (V) pentoxide, 4 hours).  

# Residue on ignition NMT $0.2\%$ (0.1 g).  

Assay Weigh accurately about $10~\mathrm{mg}$ each of Estradiol Benzoate and estradiol benzoate RS, previously dried, dissolve separately in methanol to make exactly $20~\mathrm{mL}$ Pipet $5~\mathrm{mL}$ each of these solutions, add exactly $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, then add methanol to make $20\;\mathrm{mL}$ , and use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution, respectively. Perform the test with 5 $\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and calculate the ratios, $Q_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $Q_{S}$ ,of the peak area of estradiol benzoate to that of the internal standard for the test solution and the standard solution, respectively.  

Internal standard solution —A solution of progesterone in methanol (13 in 80000).  

Operating conditions   
Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $230\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).   
Column: A stainless steel column $4~\mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $15~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography ( $5\;{\upmu\mathrm{m}}$ in particle diameter).   
Column temperature: A constant temperature of about $35\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  
Mobile phase: A mixture of acetonitrile and water $(7:3)$ .  
Flow rate: Adjust the flow rate so that the retention time of estradiol benzoate is about 10 minutes.   
System suitability   
System performance: Proceed with $5\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the  

standard solution according to the above conditions; the internal standard and estradiol benzoate are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 9.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $5~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solution as directed in the above conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratios of estradiol benzoate to the peak area of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, tight containers.  

# Estradiol Valerate 에스트라디올발레레이트  

![](images/7ee0d235a9b0ad7f630745e155a953c209e451c2639212304cd36120b1939796.jpg)  
$\mathrm{C}_{23}\mathrm{H}_{32}\mathrm{O}_{3}:356.50$  

(17β)-3-Hydroxyestra-1,3,5(10)-trien-17-yl pentanoate [979-32-8 ]  

Estradiol Valerate contains NLT $98.0\%$ and NMT $102.0\%$ of Estradiol Valerate $\left(\mathbf{C}_{23}\mathbf{H}_{32}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right)$ ).  

Description Estradiol Valerate occurs as a white crystalline powder, is odorless or has a slightly oily odor. It is soluble in castor oil, methanol, benzylbenzoate or 1,4-dioxane, sparingly soluble in sesame oil or peanut oil, and practically insoluble in water.  

Identification Determine the infrared spectra of Estradiol Valerate and estradiol valerate RS, prepared by adding chloroform and potassium bromide to Estradiol Valerate or estradiol valerate RS, then grinding and drying at 105 $^{\circ}\mathbf{C}.$ , as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibits similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $+41^{\circ}$ and $+47^{\circ}$ $\left.0.5\ \mathrm{g}\right.$ ,calculated on the anhydrous basis, methanol, $20~\mathrm{mL}$ , 100 mm).  

Melting point Between 143 and $150\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ (Method 1). Purity (1) Estradiol —Dissolve $50~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estradiol Valerate in $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of acetone and use this solution as the test solution. Separately, dissolve $5~\mathrm{mg}$ of estradiol valerate RS in $100\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of acetone and use this solution as the standard solution. With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot 5 $\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution on a plate made of silica gel for thin-layer chromatography. Next, develop the plate with a mixture of cyclohexane and ethyl acetate $(7:3)$ as the developing solvent to a distance of about $15~\mathrm{cm}$ and dry the plate at $90\;^{\circ}\!C$ for 30 minutes. Spray evenly a solution of sulfuric acid in methanol (3 in 10) on the plate and heat at $90\ ^{\circ}\mathbf{C}$ for 30 minutes; spots other than the principal spot from the test solution or the spot corresponding to estradiol are not more intense or not greater than the spots from the standard solution (NMT $1.0\%$ ).  

(2) Free acid —Neutralize $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol(95) in an Erlenmeyer flask with $0.01\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide VS to a pale blue color, using bromothymol blue TS. Weigh accurately about $0.50~\mathrm{g}$ of Estradiol Valerate and dissolve in the neutralized ethanol. Titrate with 0.01 $\mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide VS to a pale blue color. (NMT $0.5\%$ of valeric acid)  

# Each mL of $0.01\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide VS $=1.021\ \mathrm{mg}$ of $C_{5}\mathrm{H}_{10}\mathrm{O}_{2}$  

(3) Related substances —Dissolve $0.1~\mathrm{g}$ of Estradiol Valerate in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of acetone and use this solution as the test solution. Separately, weigh $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of estradiol valerate RS and add acetone to make $10~\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $0.1~\mathrm{mL}$ ,$0.5~\mathrm{mL}$ ,$1~\mathrm{mL}$ and $2~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution and add acetone to each to make exactly $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ and use these solutions as the standard solutions (1),(2), (3) and (4). With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot $20~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solutions (1), (2), (3) and (4) on a plate of silica gel for thin-layer chromatography. Develop the plate with a mixture of cyclohexane and ether $(4:1)$ as the developing solvent to a distance of about $15~\mathrm{cm}$ and air-dry the plate. Spray evenly sulfuric acid in ethanol(95) (1 in 10) on the plate, heat the plate until burn and cool. Examine under ultraviolet light (main wavelength: $254~\mathrm{nm}$ and $366~\mathrm{nm}$ ). Compare the intensities of any spot other than the principal spot from the test solution with those from the standard solution; the relative intensity is NMT $2.0\%$ .  

# Water NMT $0.1\%$ ($\mathbf{\mathcal{S}\Sigma g}$ , direct titration).  

Assay Weigh accurately about $25~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estradiol Valerate and estradiol valerate RS, dissolve each in the internal standard solution to make exactly $25\,\mathrm{\mL}$ and use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution, respectively. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the ratio of the peak area of Estradiol Valerate to that of the internal standard, $Q_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $Q_{S}$ .Internal standard solution —Testosterone benzoate solution in tetrahydrofuran (2 in 1000).  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $280\;\mathrm{nm})$ .  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4\textrm{m m}$ in internal diameter and $30\;\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography (about $5\;\mathrm{{\mum}}$ to $10\,\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: Dissolve $0.8~\mathrm{g}$ of ammonium nitrate in $300\;\mathrm{mL}$ of water, add $700\;\mathrm{mL}$ of acetonitrile and mix. Flow rate: $2\ \mathrm{mL/min}$  

System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution under the above operating conditions; estradiol valerate and the internal standard are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 3.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $10\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the above conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratio is NMT $1.5\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, tight containers.  

# Estradiol Valerate Injection 에스트라디올발레레이트주사액  

Estradiol Valerate Injection is an oily preparation for injection, and contains NLT $90.0\%$ and NMT $115.0\%$ of the labeled amount of estradiol valerate $\left(\mathbf{C}_{23}\mathbf{H}_{32}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right.$ :356.50).  

Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Injections, with Estradiol Valerate.  

Description Estradiol Valerate Injection occurs as a pale yellow distillate.  

Identification Add $0.5\ \mathrm{mL}$ of Estradiol Valerate Injection in a separatory funnel with $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of hexane and 10 $\mathrm{mL}$ of $80\%$ methanol, shake for 2 minutes to mix, and allow to stand to separate the layers. To $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of the bottom layer solution, add $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of Folin TS (dilute by adding $2~\mathrm{mL}$ of water to $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of stock solution when using) and $3\ \mathrm{mL}$ of sodium carbonate solution (1 in 5); the resulting solution exhibits a blue color.  

Purity Estradiol— Pipet an appropriate amount of Estradiol Valerate Injection according to the labeled amount, and add acetone to obtain a solution containing $30\%$ . To $1.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add the oil used in the injection to make exactly $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the estradiol solution. Perform the test with this solution and estradiol valerate injection as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot $5\,\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of these solutions on the plate made of silica gel for thin-layer chromatography. Proceed as directed under Estradiol of Estradiol Valerate (NMT $3.0\%$ ).  

Sterility Meets the requirements. Particulate contamination: Visible particles Meets the requirements.  

Insoluble particulate matter in injections Meets the requirements.  

Extractable volume of injections Meets the requirements.  

Assay Pipet an amount of Estradiol Valerate Injection equivalent to about $20~\mathrm{~mg~}$ of estradiol valerate $\left(\mathbf{C}_{23}\mathbf{H}_{32}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right)$ according to the labeled amount, wash the pipet with tetrahydrofuran, add $5.0\,\textrm{m L}$ of the internal standard solution, and then add tetrahydrofuran to make exactly $25~\mathrm{mL}$ . Use this solution as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $20~\mathrm{mg}$ of estradiol valerate RS, add $5.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, add tetrahydrofuran to make exactly $25~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test as directed in the Assay of Estradiol Valerate.  

Amount (mg) estradiol valerate $(\mathbf{C}_{23}\mathbf{H}_{32}\mathbf{O}_{3})$ )$=$ Amount (mg) of estradiol valerate $\mathrm{RS}\times\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}$ Internal standard solution —Solution of testosterone benzoate in tetrahydrofuran (8 in 1000).  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, hermetic containers.  

# Estradiol Valerate Tablets 에스트라디올발레레이트정  

Estradiol Valerate Tablets contain NLT $95.0\%$ and NMT $105.0\%$ of the labeled amount of estradiol valerate $(\mathrm{C}_{23}\mathrm{H}_{32}\mathrm{O}_{3}:356.50)$ .  

Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Tablets, with Estradiol Valerate.  

Identification Weigh an amount of Estradiol Valerate Tablets, equivalent to $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of estradiol valerate, according to the labeled amount, dissolve in $25\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of $80\%$ methanol, and filter. Use the filtrate as the test solution. Separately, weigh $10\,\mathrm{~mg}$ of estradiol valerate RS, add $80\%$ methanol to make $25~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution on the thin-layer chromatographic plate made of silica gel with fluorescent indicator for thin-layer chromatography. Next, develop the plate with a mixture of hexane and ethyl acetate $(8:2)$ as the developing solvent to a distance of about $10\;\mathrm{cm}$ , and air-dry the plate. Spray evenly the coloring agent (dissolve $20\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of toluenesulfonic acid in ethanol to make $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ ), and then examine the plate under ultraviolet light (main wavelength: 254 nm); the $R_{\mathrm{f}}$ values and the colors of the spots obtained from the test solution and the standard solution are the same.  

Disintegration Meets the requirements. Uniformity of dosage units Meets the requirements. Assay Weigh accurately the mass of NLT 20 tablets of Estradiol Valerate Tablets and powder. Weigh accurately an amount equivalent to about $2~\mathrm{mg}$ of estradiol valerate, add $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of $0.1\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ hydrochloric acid, shake to mix, and warm on a steam bath at $50~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 10 minutes. Then, add $4.0\,\textrm{m L}$ of internal standard solution, warm for 20 minutes, filter, and use the filtrate as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $0.1~\mathrm{g}$ of estradiol valerate RS and add the internal standard solution to make $200\;\mathrm{mL}$ . Take $20.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add $5.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of 0.1 $\mathrm{mol/L}$ hydrochloric acid, and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $20~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions; determine the peak area ratios, $\mathrm{Q_{T}}$ and $\mathrm{Q}_{\mathrm{S}}$ , of estradiol to the peak area of the internal standard, respectively.  

Amount (mg) of estradiol valerate $\left(\mathbf{C}_{23}\mathbf{H}_{32}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right)$ $=$ Amount (mg) of estradiol valerate $\mathrm{RS}\times\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}\times\frac{1}{50}$ Internal standard solution —A solution of diflucortolone valerate in methanol (5 in 10000).  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $280\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4.0\ \mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $30~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography (3 to $10\;\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: A mixture of methanol and water (725: 275).   
Flow rate: 2.0 mL/min  

Packaging and storage Preserve in well-closed containers.

Estriol $\mathrm{C_{18}H_{24}O_{3}}$ : 288.38 $(16\upalpha,17\upbeta)$ -Estra-1,3,5(10)-triene-3,16,17-triol [ 50-27-1 ]Estriol, when dried, contains NLT $97.0\%$ and NMT $102.0\%$ of estriol $\left(\mathbf{C}_{18}\mathbf{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right)$ .  

Description Estriol occurs as a white crystalline powder and is odorless.  

It is sparingly soluble in methanol, slightly soluble in ethanol(95) or 1,4-Dioxane and practically insoluble in water or ether.  

Identification (1) Dissolve $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estriol in $100~\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol(95) by warming, and use this solution as the test solution. Evaporate $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution on a steam bath to dryness, add $5\,\textrm{m L}$ of a solution of sodium pphenolsulfonate in phosphoric acid (1 in 50), heat at $150\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 10 minutes, and cool; the resulting solution exhibits a purple color.  

(2) Dissolve $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estriol and estriol RS in 100 mL of ethanol(95) by warming, determine the absorption spectra as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavelengths.  

(3) Determine the infrared spectra of Estriol and estriol RS, previously dried, as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $+60^{\circ}$ and $+65^{\circ}$ (after drying, $80\;\mathrm{mg}$ , ethanol(99.5), $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ ,$100\;\mathrm{mm}$ ).  

Melting point Between 281 and $286\,^{\circ}\!\mathbf{C}$ Purity (1) Heavy metals —Proceed with $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Estriol according to Method 2 and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $2.0\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of lead standard solution $(\mathrm{NMT}\,\,20\,\,\mathrm{ppm})$ ).  

(2) Related substances —Dissolve about $40~\mathrm{mg}$ of Estriol in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol(95) by warming and use this solution as the test solution. Pipet $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add ethanol(95) to make $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot $5~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution on a plate made of silica gel for thin-layer chromatography. Develop the plate with a mixture of chloroform, methanol, acetone, and acetic acid(100) ( $:18:1:1:$ 1) as the developing solvent to a distance of about $15~\mathrm{cm}$ ,and air-dry the plate. Spray evenly diluted sulfuric acid (1 in 2) on the plate and heat at $105~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 15 minutes; the spots other than the principal spot from the test solution are not more intense than the spots from the standard solution.  

# Loss on drying NMT $0.5\%$ ($0.5\;\mathrm{g}$ ,$105\;^{\circ}\!C$ , 3 hours).  

Residue on ignition NMT $0.1\%$ (0.5 g). Assay Weigh accurately the average about $25~\mathrm{mg}$ each of Estriol and estriol RS, previously dried, dissolve separately in methanol to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $10~\mathrm{mL}$ each of these solutions, add exactly $5\ \mathrm{ml}$ of the internal standard solution, add methanol to make $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ , and use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution, respectively. Perform the test with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and determine the ratio of the peak area of Estriol to that of the internal standard, $Q_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $Q_{\mathrm{S}}$ .  

# Amount (mg) of estriol $(\mathbf{C}_{18}\mathbf{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{3})$ )$=$ Amount (mg) of estriol $\mathrm{RS}{\times}\,\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}$  

Internal standard solution —A solution of methyl benzoate in methanol (1 in 1000).  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $280\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4\,\textrm{m m}$ in internal diameter and $15~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with octadecylsilanized silica gel for liquid chromatography ( $\ensuremath{\left\langle5\;\ensuremath{\upmu\mathrm{m}}\right.\right.}$ in particle diameter).  

Column temperature: A constant temperature of about $25\ ^{\circ}\mathbf{C}$ .  

Mobile phase: A mixture of water and methanol (51:49).  

Flow rate: Adjust the flow rate so that the retention time of Estriol is about 10 minutes.  

System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution under the above operating conditions; estriol and the internal standard are eluted in this order with the resolution being NLT 8.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution under the above operating conditions; the relative standard deviation of the peak area ratios of estriol to that of the internal standard is NMT $1.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in tight containers.  

# Estriol Tablets 에스트리올정  

Estriol Tablets contain NLT $90.0\%$ and NMT $110.0\%$ of the labeled amount of estriol $\left(\mathrm{C}_{18}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathrm{O}_{3}\ :\right.$ 288.38).  

Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Tablets, with Estriol.  

Identification Weigh an amount of Estriol Tablets, previously powdered, equivalent to $2~\mathrm{mg}$ of estriol according to the labeled amount, add $20\,\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol(95), shake to mix for 10 minutes, and centrifuge. Use the clear supernatant as the test solution. Perform the Identification (1) and (2) of Estriol with the test solution.  

Dissolution Perform the test with 1 tablet of Estriol Tablets at 50 revolutions per minute according to Method 2 under the Dissolution, using $900~\mathrm{mL}$ of water as the dissolution medium. Take NLT $20\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the dissolved solution 30 minutes after starting the test, and filter through a membrane filter with a pore size of NMT $0.8~{\upmu\mathrm{m}}$ . Discard the first $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of the filtrate, pipet $\mathrm{~V~mL~}$ of the subsequent filtrate, add water to make exactly $\mathrm{V}^{\circ}\,\,\mathrm{mL}$ of solution containing about $0.1~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ of estriol $\left(\mathbf{C}_{18}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right)$ per mL according to the labeled amount, and use this solution as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about 10 mg of estriol RS, previously dried at $105~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 3 hours, and dissolve in methanol to make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $5\ \mathrm{mL}$ of this solution and add water to make $100\ \mathrm{mL}$ .Pipet $2~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add water to make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $100~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution according to the operating conditions under the Assay of Estriol, and measure the peak areas, $\mathrm{A_{T}}$ and $\mathrm{A}_{\mathrm{S}}$ , of estriol, respectively.  

It meets the requirements when the dissolution rate of Estriol Tablets in 30 minutes is NLT $80\%$ .  

Dissolution rate $(\%)$ of the labeled amount of estriol  

$$
\begin{array}{c}{{(\mathrm{C}_{18}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathrm{O}_{3})}}\\ {{=W_{\mathrm{S}}\times\displaystyle\frac{A_{\mathrm{T}}}{A_{\mathrm{S}}}\times\displaystyle\frac{V^{\prime}}{V}\times\displaystyle\frac{1}{\mathrm{C}}\times\displaystyle\frac{9}{10}}}\end{array}
$$  

# $W_{\mathrm{S}}$ : Amount (mg) of estriol RS  

$C$ : Labeled amount (mg) of estriol $\left(\mathbf{C}_{18}\mathbf{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right)$ ) in 1 tablet  

Uniformity of dosage units It meets the requirements when the Content uniformity test is performed according to the following procedure. Take 1 tablet of Estriol Tablets, add exactly $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of water, sonicate to disperse, and add exactly $15\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of methanol. Shake to mix for 15 minutes. Centrifuge this solution for 10 minutes, pipet a certain amount of the clear supernatant, and add methanol to obtain a solution having known concentration of about $5~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ of estriol $\left(\mathbf{C}_{18}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right)$ per mL. Pipet $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add exactly $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, and use this solution as the test solution. Perform the test solution with $20~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the test solution under the Assay of Estriol as follow. However, prepare the internal standard solution with a solution of methyl benzoate in methanol (1 in 40000). Measure the average value from the peak area ratios of individual 10 tablets of Estriol Tablets; it meets the requirements when the deviation $(\%)$ between the value and the individual peak area ratio is within $15\%$ . Also, perform the test with another 20 tablets of Estriol Tablets when there is 1 tablet with a deviation $(\%)$ of more than $15\%$ and less than $25\%$ . Calculate the deviation $(\%)$ between the average value of total 30 tablets from the two tests and each peak area ratio; it meets the requirements when there is NMT 1 tablet with a deviation of more than $15\%$ and less than $25\%$ , and there are no tablets with a deviation of more than $25\%$ .Assay Weigh accurately NLT 20 tablets of Estriol Tablets, and powder. Weigh accurately an amount equivalent to about $1~\mathrm{mg}$ of estriol $\left(\mathbf{C}_{18}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{3}\right)$ , add exactly $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of water, sonicate to disperse, and add $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol. Shake to mix for 10 minutes, centrifuge, and take the clear supernatant. Add $25\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of methanol, repeat the procedure 2 times in the same manner, combine the clear supernatant, and add $5.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, and add methanol to make exactly $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ . Use this solution as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $25~\mathrm{mg}$ of estriol RS, previously dried at $105\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 3 hours, and dissolve in methanol to make exactly 100 mL. Pipet $4\;\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add $5.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the internal standard solution, add methanol to make exactly 100 mL, and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with exactly $20~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution under the Assay of Estriol.  

$$
\begin{array}{c}{{\mathrm{Amount}\ (\mathrm{mg})\ \mathrm{of}\ \mathrm{estriol}\ (\mathrm{C}_{18}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathrm{O}_{3})}}\\ {{=\mathrm{Amount}\ (\mathrm{mg})\ \mathrm{of}\ \mathrm{estriol}\ \mathrm{RS}\times{\frac{Q_{\mathrm{T}}}{Q_{\mathrm{S}}}}\times{\frac{1}{25}}}}\end{array}
$$  

Internal standard solution —A solution of methyl benzoate in methanol (1 in 5000).  

Packaging and storage Preserve in tight containers. Etacrynic Acid $\mathrm{C}_{13}\mathrm{H}_{12}\mathrm{Cl}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{4}$ : 303.14 [2,3-Dichloro-4-(2-methylenebutanoyl)phenoxy]acetic acid [ 58-54-8 ]  

![](images/56e101916bd52a43c8cc29a343eab69ea56fa470012d0e159bf30ad29a194867.jpg)  

Etacrynic Acid, when dried, contains NLT 98.0 and NMT $101.0\%$ of etacrynic acid $(\mathbf{C}_{13}\mathbf{H}_{12}\mathbf{C}\mathrm{l}_{2}\mathbf{O}_{4})$ ).  

Description Etacrynic Acid occurs as a white, crystalline powder. It is odorless and has a slightly bitter taste. It is very soluble in methanol, freely soluble in ethanol(95), acetic acid(100) and ether, and very slightly soluble in water.  

Identification (1) Dissolve $0.2\:\mathrm{g}$ of Etacrynic Acid in 10 mL of acetic acid(100), and to $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add $0.1~\mathrm{mL}$ of bromine TS; the color of the test solution disappears. To the remaining $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of the solution, add 0.1 mL of potassium permanganate TS; the color of the test solution immediately changes to light orange.  

(2) Add $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of sodium hydroxide TS to $0.01\ \mathrm{g}$ of Etacrynic Acid, and heat on a steam bath for 3 minutes. After cooling, add $1\ \mathrm{mL}$ of chromotropic acid TS, and heat on a steam bath for 10 minutes; the solution exhibits an intense purple color.  

(3) Determine the absorption spectra of solutions of Etacrynic Acid and etacrynic acid RS in methanol (1 in 20000) as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavelengths.  

(4) Perform the test with Etacrynic Acid as directed under the Flame Coloration (2); it exhibits a green color.  

# Melting point Between 121 and $125~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$  

Purity (1) Clarity and color of solution— Dissolve $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Etacrynic Acid in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol; the solution is clear and colorless.  

(2) Heavy metals— Proceed with $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Etacrynic Acid according to Method 4 and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $2.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of lead standard solution $(\mathrm{NMT}\,\,20\,\,\mathrm{ppm})$ ).  

(3) Arsenic —Proceed with $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Etacrynic Acid according to Method 3 and perform the test. Add $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of a solution of magnesium nitrate hexahydrate in ethanol(95) (1 in 50), then add $1.5\ \mathrm{mL}$ of hydrogen peroxide(30), and fire to burn $(\mathrm{NMT}\,\,2\,\,\mathrm{ppm}$ ).  

(4) Related substances —Dissolve about $0.20\ \mathrm{g}$ of Etacrynic Acid in $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol(95) and use this solution as the test solution. Pipet $3\ \mathrm{mL}$ of this solution, add ethanol(95) to make exactly $200~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot $10~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution on the thin-layer chromatographic plate made of silica gel with fluorescent indicator for thin-layer chromatography. Next, develop the plate with a mixture of chloroform, ethyl acetate, and acetic acid(100) $(6:5:$ 2) as the developing solvent to a distance of about $15\;\mathrm{cm}$ ,and air-dry the plate. Examine the plate under ultraviolet light (main wavelength: $254\;\mathrm{nm}$ ); the spots other than the principal spot from the test solution are not more intense than the spots from the standard solution.  

Loss on drying NMT $0.25\%$ ($1\ \mathrm{g}_{}$ , in vacuum, $60~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}_{!}$ , 2 hours).  

# Residue on ignition NMT $0.1\%$ ($\mathrm{~\ensuremath~{~1~}~}\mathrm{g})$  

Assay Weigh accurately about $0.1\ \mathrm{g}$ of Etacrynic Acid, previously dried, put in an iodine bottle, dissolve in 20 mL of acetic acid(100), and add exactly $20~\mathrm{mL}$ of 0.05 $\mathrm{mol/L}$ bromine. To this solution, add $3\ \mathrm{mL}$ of hydrochloric acid, stopper tightly at once, shake, and allow to stand in a dark place for 60 minutes. Then, carefully add $50~\mathrm{mL}$ of water and $15\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of potassium iodide TS, stopper tightly immediately, shake well, and titrate the liberated iodine with $0.1\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium thiosulfate VS (indicator: 1 mL of starch TS). Perform a blank test in the same manner and make any necessary correction.  

Packaging and storage Preserve in well-closed containers.  

# Ethambutol Hydrochloride 에탐부톨염산염  

![](images/47a3e625afeca5df2882a903558206ca7a657db923d73a2f7ac9bfd51a5598b0.jpg)  
$\mathrm{C}_{10}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathrm{N}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{2}.$ ·2HCl: 277.23  

$(2S,2^{\circ}S)–2,2^{\circ}$ -(Ethane-1,2-diyldiimino)dibutan-1-ol dihydrochloride [ 1070-11-7 ]  

Ethambutol Hydrochloride, when dried, contains NLT $98.5\%$ and NMT $101.0\%$ of ethambutol hydrochloride $\mathrm{\bf\left(C_{10}H_{24}N_{2}O_{2}\cdot2H C l\right)}$ ).  

Description Ethambutol Hydrochloride occurs as white crystals or a crystalline powder, is odorless and has a bitter taste.  

It is very soluble in water, soluble in methanol and in ethanol(95), and practically insoluble in ether. The pH of a solution of Ethambutol Hydrochloride (1 in 20) in $20\;\mathrm{mL}$ of water is between 3.4 and 4.0.  

Identification (1) Determine the infrared spectra of Ethambutol Hydrochloride and ethambutol hydrochloride RS, previously dried, as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

(2) An aqueous solution of Ethambutol Hydrochloride (1 in 30) responds to the Qualitative Analysis for chloride.  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $+5.5$ and $+6.1^{\circ}$ (after drying, $5.0\;\mathrm{g}$ , water, $50\;\mathrm{mL}$ ,$200\;\mathrm{mm}$ ).  

Melting point Between $200\,^{\circ}\!C$ and $204\,^{\circ}\!C$ Purity (1) Clarity and color of solution —Dissolve $1.0\;\mathrm{g}$ of Ethambutol Hydrochloride in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of water; the solution is clear and colorless.  

(2) Heavy metals— Proceed with $2.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Ethambutol Hydrochloride according to Method 1 and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $2.0\,\mathrm{~mL~}$ of lead standard solution (NMT 10 ppm).  

(3) Arsenic —Prepare the test solution with $1.0~\mathrm{g}$ of Ethambutol Hydrochloride, according to Method 1 and perform the test (NMT 2 ppm).  

(4) Related substances —Dissolve $0.10~\mathrm{g}$ of Ethambutol Hydrochloride in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol and use this solution as the test solution. Separately, dissolve $2~\mathrm{mg}$ of ethambutol hydrochloride RS in $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of methanol, and use this solution as the standard solution. With these solutions, perform the test as directed under the Thin Layer Chromatography. Spot $20~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution on a plate made of silica gel for thin-layer chromatography. Develop the plate with a mixture of methanol and ammonia water(28) $(18:1)$ as the developing solvent to a distance of about $15~\mathrm{cm}$ , and airdry the plate. Spray evenly iodine chloroform solution TS for spray on the plate; the spots other than the principal spots from the test solution are not more intense than the spots from the standard solution $(2.0\%)$ .  

(5) 2-Aminobutanol —Weigh accurately about 50 mg of Ethambutol Hydrochloride, dissolve in water to make exactly $100\,\mathrm{\mL}$ and use this solution as the test solution.  Separately, dissolve adequate amount of 2- aminobutanol RS, weighed accurately, in water and dilute sequentially to make a solution containing $5~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ per mL and use this solution as the standard solution. Transfer 10 mL of the test solution into a $100{\-}\mathrm{mL}$ Erlenmeyer flask with glass stopper and add $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of water and $20~\mathrm{mL}$ of boric acid buffer solution. Separately, mix $10.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the test solution, $10.0\ \mathrm{mL}$ of the standard solution, and 20 mL of boric acid buffer solution in a $100{\-}\mathrm{mL}$ Erlenmeyer flask. While the contents in two flasks are mixed on shaker, quickly add $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of fluorescamine solution and stopper them and mix briefly. Perform the test after exactly 1 minute with these solutions as directed under the Fluorescence Spectroscopy. Determine the fluorescence intensity at $385~\mathrm{nm}$ of excitation wavelength and $485~\mathrm{nm}$ of emission wavelength: the fluorescence intensity obtained from the test solution is NMT that of the difference between two solutions (NMT $1.0\%$ ).  

Boric acid buffer solution —Weigh about $1.24\mathrm{~g~}$ of boric acid, dissolve in $90\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of water, adjust with 5 $\mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide to $\mathrm{pH}\,9.0$ , and dilute with water to exactly $100\;\mathrm{mL}$ and mix.  

Fluorescamine solution —Transfer $5~\mathrm{\mg}$ of fluorescamine into a cylinder with stopper and scale line, and dissolve in $50\;\mathrm{mL}$ of acetone.  

Loss on drying NMT $0.5\%$ (1 $\mathsf{g},\,105\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ , 3 hours). Residue on ignition NMT $0.1\%$ (1 g). Assay Weigh accurately about $0.2{\mathrm{~g~}}$ of Ethambutol Hydrochloride, previously dried, dissolve in $50\;\mathrm{mL}$ of water, add $1\ \mathrm{mL}$ of $0.1\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ hydrochloric acid TS and titrate with $0.1\ \mathrm{\mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide TS from the first equivalence point to the second equivalence point (potentiometric titration under the Titrimetry).  

Each mL of $0.1\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide VS  $=27.723~\mathrm{mg}$ of $\mathrm{C}_{10}\mathrm{H}_{24}\mathrm{N}_{2}\mathrm{O}_{2}$ ·2HCl  

Packaging and storage Preserve in tight containers.  

# Ethambutol Hydrochloride Tablets 에탐부톨염산염정  

Ethambutol Hydrochloride Tablets contain NLT $95.0\%$ and NMT $105.0\%$ of the labeled amount of eth  

ambutol hydrochloride $(\mathrm{C_{10}H_{24}N_{2}O_{2}}{\cdot}2\mathrm{HCl}:277.23)$  

# Method of preparation Prepare as directed under Tablets, with Ethambutol Hydrochloride.  

Identification (1) Weigh an amount of Ethambutol Hydrochloride Tablets, previously powdered, equivalent to $0.1\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of ethambutol hydrochloride, according to the labeled amount, add $3\ \mathrm{mL}$ of methanol, transfer into a glass mortar, and stir to mix. Again, add $5\ \mathrm{mL}$ of methanol make a suspension, and filter through a filter paper, previously moistened with methanol. Transfer the filtrate to a beaker containing $100~\mathrm{mL}$ of acetone, stir to mix, allow to stand for 15 minutes, and extract crystals. Discard the clear supernatant by inclining the container, and air-dry the crystals until there is no methanol odor. Determine the infrared spectra of these crystals and ethambutol hydrochloride RS as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit maxima at the same wavenumber.  

(2) An aqueous solution of the crystals (1 in 10), obtained from (1), responds to the Qualitative Analysis for chloride.  

Purity 2-Aminobutanol —Take an appropriate number of tablets, equivalent to $400~\mathrm{mg}$ of ethambutol hydrochloride, transfer in a beaker, add acetone until the tablets are submerged, and allow to stand for 15 minutes. Discard the acetone, then dry, powder the tablet with the coating removed, and add methanol, shake to mix, make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ , and filter. Pipet $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of the filtrate, and dilute with water to make exactly $200~\mathrm{mL}$ . Allow to stand for 15 minutes, filter through a dried filter paper, discard the first turbid filtrate, and use the subsequent filtrate as the test solution. Proceed with this solution under the Purity (5) of Ethambutol Hydrochloride.  

Dissolution Perform the test with 1 tablet of Ethambutol Hydrochloride Tablets at 100 revolutions per minute according to Method 1 under the Dissolution, using $900\;\mathrm{mL}$ of water as the dissolution medium. Take the dissolved solution 45 minutes after starting the test, filter, and use the filtrate as the test solution. Separately, weigh an appropriate amount of ethambutol hydrochloride RS, previously dried at $105\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 2 hours, dissolve in water to make a solution containing $0.1~\mathrm{mg}$ per mL, and use this solution as the standard solution. Transfer $1~\mathrm{mL}$ each of the test solution, the standard solution and water to 3 glass-stoppered centrifuge tubes, add $5.0~\mathrm{mL}$ of bromocresol green solution and $10.0\ \mathrm{mL}$ of chloroform, respectively, close with the stoppers, and shake vigorously to mix. Allow to stand until the chloroform layer separates, discard the supernatant water layer, and filter the chloroform layer through cotton. Perform the test with these solutions as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy, and measure the absorbance at the absorbance maximum wavelength at about $415~\mathrm{nm}$ .  

The acceptable dissolution criterion of Ethambutol Hydrochloride Tablets is NLT $75\%$ (Q) dissolved in 45 Phosphate buffer solution —Dissolve $38.0~\mathrm{g}$ of sodium dihydrogen phosphate dihydrate and $2.0\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of anhydrous sodium dihydrogen phosphate in water to make $1000\,\mathrm{mL}$ .  

Bromocresol green solution —Weigh $0.2\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of bromocresol green, dissolve in $30~\mathrm{mL}$ of water and $6.5~\mathrm{mL}$ of $0.1\;\mathrm{\mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide, add phosphate buffer solution to make $500~\mathrm{mL}$ , and mix. Then, add $0.1\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ hydrochloric acid to adjust the $\mathrm{pH}$ to $4.6\pm0.1$ .  

# Uniformity of dosage units Meets the requirements.  

Assay Weigh accurately NLT 20 tablets of Ethambutol Hydrochloride Tablets, and powder. Weigh accurately about 30 mg of ethambutol hydrochloride $\mathrm{(C_{10}H_{24}N_{2}O_{2}{\cdot}2H C l)}$ , dissolve in water by shaking to mix, then add water to make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ , and filter. Discard the first $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of the filtrate, and use the subsequent filtrate as the test solution. Separately, weigh accurately about $30~\mathrm{mg}$ of ethambutol hydrochloride RS, dissolve in water to make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ , and use this solution as the standard solution. Perform the test with $50~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the test solution and the standard solution as directed under the Liquid Chromatography according to the following conditions, and measure the peak areas, $A_{\mathrm{T}}$ and $A_{S}$ , of ethambutol hydrochloride in each solution.  

Amount $\left(\mathrm{mg}\right)$ of ethambutol hydrochloride $\mathrm{(C_{10}H_{24}N_{2}O_{2}{\cdot}2H C l)}$  

$=$ Amount (mg) of ethambutol hydrochloride $\mathrm{RS}\!\times\!\frac{A_{\mathrm{T}}}{A_{\mathrm{S}}}$  

Operating conditions  

Detector: An ultraviolet absorption photometer (wavelength: $200\;\mathrm{nm}$ ).  

Column: A stainless steel column about $4.6~\mathrm{mm}$ in internal diameter and about $15~\mathrm{cm}$ in length, packed with nitrile silica gel for liquid chromatography ( $5\;\upmu\mathrm{m}$ in particle diameter).  

Mobile phase: A mixture of a solution, obtained by mixing $1.0\;\mathrm{mL}$ of triethylamine and $1000~\mathrm{mL}$ of water to adjust the $\mathrm{pH}$ to 7.0 with phosphoric acid, and acetonitrile $(1:1)$ .  

Flow rate: $1.0\,\mathrm{mL/min}$ System suitability  

System performance: Proceed with $50~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ of the standard solution according to the conditions above; the symmetry factor is NMT 2.0.  

System repeatability: Repeat the test 6 times with $50~\upmu\mathrm{L}$ each of the standard solution according to the conditions above; the relative standard deviation of the peak areas of ethambutol hydrochloride is NMT $2.0\%$ .  

Packaging and storage Preserve in well-closed containers.  

# Ethenzamide 에텐자미드  

![](images/3dc72fb93fc6bec6d67a926d8f03ea4dc11ffcbcc36ae5d7439ba1f02d24612f.jpg)  

2-Ethoxybenzamide $\mathrm{C}_{9}\mathrm{H}_{11}\mathrm{NO}_{2}$ : 165.19 2-Ethoxybenzamide [ 938-73-8 ]  
Ethenzamide, when dried, contains NLT $98.0\%$ and NMT $101\%$ of ethenzamide $\left(\mathrm{C}\mathrm{{sH}_{11}}\mathrm{{NO}_{2}}\right)$ .Description Ethenzamide occurs as white crystals or a crystalline powder.   
It is soluble in methanol, ethanol(95) or acetone and practically insoluble in water.   
It begins to sublime slightly at about $105\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  

Identification (1) Take $0.5~\mathrm{g}$ of Ethenzamide, add $5~\mathrm{mL}$ of sodium hydroxide TS and heat the mixture gently; the gas produced turns moistened red litmus paper to blue. (2) Take $0.2{\mathrm{~g~}}$ of Ethenzamide, add $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of hydrobromic acid and boil the mixture gently for 1 hour under a reflux condenser. Cool in ice-water, filter and collect the separated crystalline precipitate, wash 3 times with $5~\mathrm{mL}$ each of ice-water and dry in a desiccator (in vacuum, silica gel) for 2 hours; the precipitate melts between $158\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ and $161\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  

(3) Determine the absorption spectra of solutions of Ethenzamide and ethenzamide RS in methanol (1 in 100000) as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavelengths.  

(4) Determine the infrared spectra of Ethenzamide and ethenzamide RS, previously dried, as directed in the potassium bromide disk method under the Mid-infrared Spectroscopy; both spectra exhibit similar intensities of absorption at the same wavenumbers.  

Melting point Between 131 and $134\,^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .Purity (1) Chloride —Dissolve $0.5~\mathrm{g}$ of Ethenzamide in $30~\mathrm{mL}$ of acetone, add $6\;\mathrm{mL}$ of dilute nitric acid and water to make $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Use this solution as the test solution and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with 0.7 $\mathrm{mL}$ of $0.01\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ hydrochloric acid, $30\;\mathrm{mL}$ of acetone, 6 mL of dilute nitric acid and water to make $50~\mathrm{mL}$ (NMT $0.050\%$ ).  

(2) Sulfate —Dissolve $0.5\ \mathrm{g}$ of Ethenzamide in 30 mL of acetone and add $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of dilute hydrochloric acid and water to make $50~\mathrm{mL}$ . Use this solution as the test solution and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $0.50~\mathrm{mL}$ of $0.005\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ sulfuric acid, add $30~\mathrm{mL}$ of acetone, $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of dilute hydrochloric acid and water to 50  

mL (NMT $0.048\%$  

(3) Heavy metals —Proceed with $2.0\,\mathrm{~g~}$ of Ethenzamide according to Method 2 and perform the test. Prepare the control solution with $2.0\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of lead standard solution (NMT $10\,\mathrm{ppm})$ ).  

(4) Arsenic —Take $0.40~\mathrm{g}$ of Ethenzamide, add $0.3~\mathrm{g}$ of potassium nitrate and $0.5~\mathrm{g}$ of anhydrous sodium carbonate, mix thoroughly, ignite the mixture gradually. After cooling, dissolve the residue in $10\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of dilute sulfuric acid and heat the solution until white fumes are produced. After cooling, add water carefully to make 5 mL. Use this solution as the test solution (NMT 5 ppm). (5) Salicylamide —Dissolve $0.20~\mathrm{g}$ of Ethenzamide in $15\;\mathrm{mL}$ of dilute ethanol (2 in 3) and add 2 to 3 drops of dilute iron(III) chloride TS; the resulting solution does not exhibit a purple color.  

Loss on drying NMT $1.0\%$ ($1~\mathrm{g}$ , silica gel, 3 hours).  

# Residue on ignition NMT $0.1\%$ (1 g).  

Assay Weigh accurately about $20~\mathrm{mg}$ each of Ethenzamide and ethenzamide RS, previously dried, and dissolve each in $70~\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol(95) by warming.  After cooling, add ethanol(95) to make exactly $100~\mathrm{mL}$ . Pipet $5.0~\mathrm{mL}$ each of these solutions, add ethanol(95) to make exactly $50~\mathrm{mL}$ and use these solutions as the test solution and the standard solution, respectively.  Determine the absorbances, $\mathrm{A_{T}}$ and $\mathrm{A}_{\mathrm{S}}$ of the test solution and the standard solution, respectively, at ${290}\,\mathrm{nm}$ as directed under the Ultraviolet-visible Spectroscopy, using ethanol(95) as the blank.  

Amount (mg) of ethenzamide $\left(\boldsymbol{\mathbf{C}}\boldsymbol{\mathbf{{j}}}\mathbf{H}_{11}\boldsymbol{\mathbf{N}}\boldsymbol{\mathbf{O}}_{2}\right)$ )$=$ Amount (mg) of ethenzamide $\mathrm{RS}\!\times\!\frac{A_{\mathrm{T}}}{A_{\mathrm{S}}}$ Packaging and storage Preserve in well-closed containers.  

# Anesthetic Ether 마취용에테르  

$$
\mathsf{C H}_{3}\mathsf{C H}_{2}\mathsf{O C H}_{2}\mathsf{C H}_{3}
$$  

$\mathrm{C_{4}H_{10}O:74.12}$  

Anesthetic Ether contains NLT $96.0\%$ and NMT $98.0\%$ (by specific gravity) of ether $\left(\boldsymbol{\mathbf{C}}_{4}\boldsymbol{\mathbf{H}}_{10}\boldsymbol{\mathbf{O}}\right)$ .Anesthetic Ether contains small quantities of ethanol(95) and water, and suitable stabilizers may be added. Anesthetic Ether is not to be used for anesthesia if it has been removed from the original container for more than 24 hours.  

Description Anesthetic Ether occurs as a colorless, clear, mobile liquid, and has a characteristic odor.  

It is miscible with ethanol(95).   
It is soluble in water.   
It is highly volatile and flammable.   
It is slowly oxidized by the action of air and light, producing peroxides.   
The vapor of Anesthetic Ether, when mixed with air and ignited, may explode violently.   
Boiling point —Between 35 and $37\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  

Specific gravity $d_{20}^{20}$ : Between 0.718 and 0.721. Purity (1) Characteristic odor —Put $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of Anesthetic Ether in an evaporating dish and allow it to evaporate spontaneously to a volume of $1\,\textrm{m L}$ ; no characteristic odor is perceptible. Pour the remaining solution onto a piece of clean, odorless filter paper to evaporate ether; no characteristic odor is perceptible.  

(2) Acid —Put $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of diluted ethanol(4 in 5) and $0.5~\mathrm{mL}$ of phenolphthalein TS in a glass-stoppered flask and add $0.02\mathrm{\mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide VS dropwise to produce a red color which persists for 30 seconds after mixing by shaking. To this solution, add $25~\mathrm{mL}$ of Anesthetic Ether, stopper the flask, shake gently, and add 0.40 mL of $0.02\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide VS while mixing by shaking; a red color develops.  

(3) Aldehyde —To $100\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of water in a glassstoppered flask, add $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of Anesthetic Ether and $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of a solution of sodium bisulfite (1 in 1000), stopper tightly, shake vigorously for 10 seconds, and allow the mixture to stand in a cool place for 30 minutes, protected from light. Then, add $2\ \mathrm{mL}$ of starch TS and add 0.01 $\mathrm{mol/L}$ iodine VS dropwise until a pale blue color appears. To this solution, add about $2\mathrm{~g~}$ of sodium bicarbonate, shake to mix until the blue color disappears, and add 1 mL of diluted $0.01\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ iodine VS (9 in 40); the solution turns blue. Keep the temperature of the solution below $18\,^{\circ}\!C$ during the procedure.  

(4) Peroxide —Put $10~\mathrm{mL}$ of Anesthetic Ether in a Nessler tube, add $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of a freshly prepared solution of potassium iodide (1 in 10), allow to stand for 1 hour while shaking occasionally and protecting from light, then add $1~\mathrm{mL}$ of starch TS, and shake well to mix; no color is produced in the aqueous layer and in the ether layer.  

(5) Residue on evaporation —Evaporate $50~\mathrm{mL}$ of Anesthetic Ether and dry the residue at $105\;^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ for 1 hour; the weight of the residue is NMT $1.0~\mathrm{mg}$ .  

Water NMT $0.2\%$ $\mathrm{[0.1~\,g}$ , volumetric titration, direct titration).  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, tight containers at a temperature not exceeding $25~^{\circ}\!C$ , without filling up and protected from fire.  

# Ethinylestradiol 에티닐에스트라디올  

![](images/6049dbd910b2e4f12e03671fb6e481c8cdb1448ee86770f52ab010fa07f61b1a.jpg)  

${\bf C}_{20}{\bf H}_{24}{\bf O}_{2}$ : 296.40  

19-Nor- $17\upalpha$ -pregna-1,3,5(10)-trien-20-yne-3,17-diol [57-  
63-6 ]  

Ethinylestradiol, when dried, contains NLT $98.0\%$ and NMT $101.0\%$ of ethinylestradiol $\left(\mathbf{C}_{20}\mathbf{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{2}\right)$ .  

Description Ethinylestradiol occurs as white or pale yellow crystals or a crystalline powder and is odorless. It is freely soluble in pyridine and tetrahydrofuran, soluble in ethanol(95) and ether, and practically insoluble in water.  

It dissolves in sodium hydroxide TS. Identification (1) Dissolve $2~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ethinylestradiol in 1 mL of a mixture of sulfuric acid and ethanol(95) $(1:1)$ ;the solution exhibits a purplish red color with yellowish green fluorescence. Carefully add $2~\mathrm{mL}$ of water to this solution; the color of the solution changes to reddish purple.  

(2) Transfer $20~\mathrm{{mg}}$ of Ethinylestradiol to a glass stoppered test tube, dissolve in $10\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of a solution of potassium hydroxide (1 in 20), add $0.1~\mathrm{g}$ of benzoyl chloride, and shake. Collect the resulting precipitate by filtering. Recrystallize from methanol, and dry in a desiccator (in vacuum, phosphorus (V) pentoxide); the precipitate melts between 200 and $202~^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ .  

Optical rotation $[\alpha]_{\mathrm{D}}^{20}$ : Between $-26^{\circ}$ and $-31^{\circ}$ (after drying, $0.1~\mathrm{g}$ , pyridine, $25~\mathrm{mL}$ ,$100\;\mathrm{mm}$ ).  

Melting point Between 180 and $186\ ^{\circ}\mathrm{C}$ or 142 and $146\,^{\circ}\!C$ .  

Purity Estrone —Dissolve $5~\mathrm{mg}$ of Ethinylestradiol in $0.5\ \ \mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol(95), and add $50~\mathrm{~mg}$ of mdinitrobenzene. Add $0.5\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of freshly prepared dilute potassium hydroxide-ethanol TS, allow to stand in a dark place for 1 hour, and add $10\;\mathrm{mL}$ of ethanol(95); the color of the solution is no more intense than that of the following control solution.  

Control solution —Proceed in the same manner in the preparation of the test solution, omitting Ethinylestradiol.  

Loss on drying NMT $0.5\%$ ($\mathrm{\Delta}[0.5~\mathrm{g}$ , in vacuum, phosphorus pentoxide, 4 hours).  

Assay Weigh accurately about $0.2{\mathrm{~g~}}$ of Ethinylestradiol, previously dried, dissolve in $40\,\textrm{m L}$ of tetrahydrofuran, add $10\,\mathrm{\mL}$ of a solution of silver nitrate (1 in 20) and titrate with $0.1\ \mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide VS (potentiometric titration under the Titrimetry). Perform a blank test in the same manner, and make any necessary correction. Each mL of $0.1\;\mathrm{mol/L}$ sodium hydroxide VS $=29.640\ \mathrm{mg}$ of ${\bf C}_{20}{\bf H}_{24}{\bf O}_{2}$  

Packaging and storage Preserve in light-resistant, tight containers.  

# Ethinylestradiol Tablets 에티닐에스트라디올정

Separately, weigh accurately about $10~\mathrm{mg}$ of ethinylestradiol RS, previously dried in a desiccator (in vacuum, phosphorus pentoxide) for 4 hours, dissolve in methanol to obtain a solution containing about $0.04~\upmu\mathrm{g}$ of ethinylestradiol $(\mathbf{C}_{20}\mathbf{H}_{24}\mathbf{O}_{2})$ ) per mL, and use this solution as the standard solution. To the glass-stoppered test tubes T, S and B, put exactly $4\;\mathrm{mL}$ of sulfuric acid-methanol TS, respectively, cool with ice, add exactly $1~\mathrm{mL}$ each of the test solution, the standard solution and methanol, and shake immediately.
